1)
The Significance of the Second 7-Year Course
<Summary of the Words> Jesus had a mission to fulfill all historical responsibilities. Therefore, Jesus had to become the representative of Jacob and Moses and be the historical fruit. To do this, he had to create a boundary with the twelve apostles on behalf of Adam's family and establish a new tribal organization centered on the tribes of Israel globally. This was the mission of Jesus who came to this earth. 
The mission of Jesus and the mission of the Teacher
However, because this was not accomplished, there was resentment towards God, Jesus, and the Holy Spirit, and there was resentment among many spirits and countless people on earth. Therefore, the returning Lord must resolve all this resentment. 
Jesus, who was disbelieved by three disciples, stood in the position of Adam who lost Cain, Abel, and Seth in Adam's family, that is, in the position of the fallen human ancestor Adam, which allowed Satan to invade at will. Therefore, he could not avoid being crucified. 
Then what should the Teacher do? He must indemnify these historical facts. He must embrace the historical circumstances and restore everything. This was said on August 13, 1968 (Tuesday), at the Daegu Church. 
* This speech was given in Daegu during a nationwide tour in the first summer evangelistic period of the Second 7-Year Course, and it is published in the 15th issue (August 1968) and the 16th issue (September and October 1968) of <Gisu>. The title was added by the editor.

The significance of the Second 7-Year Course
When viewed from the position of Korea, which is in a heavenly position, Korea is in the position of Israel. Furthermore, Korean Christianity is in the same position as ancient Judaism, and America is in the position of Rome. 
If Israel had centered on Judaism and become one with Jesus, Rome would have been conquered before Jesus in a short time, and the world restoration could have been easily achieved. However, because this was not accomplished and he died on the cross, God's providence has been extended until now. 
Now, when looking at Korea today, if Korea, Christianity, and the Teacher had become one, there would be no problem in becoming one with America. If we can become one with America, we can subdue the Soviet Communist Party. 
Two thousand years ago, because Jesus, Judaism, and Israel could not become one, Jesus was driven out to the Gentiles and, even after escaping death and returning, he ultimately had to die. Therefore, Korea must indemnify and restore this, but it could not. That is why the Teacher and Korea had to separate. Therefore, it was unavoidable to return to the starting point and fight. 
The Teacher crossed over from the North and established the Unification Church instead of Christianity. If Korea and the Unification Church become one, it will be in the position of restoring what Jesus was pushed into by Judaism. The Teacher took 21 years to lay the foundation for this restoration. 
In other words, it has established the position of Jacob returning from Haran, subduing his brother Esau, and starting a new providence after 21 years. The 7-Year Course was extended to take 21 years. 
Now is the time when churches and nations, and worlds are confronting each other. However, the two worlds of democracy and communism are beginning to break. 
The reason for establishing Parents' Day, Children's Day, All Things Day, and God's Day
Because Adam and Eve fell, they could not become the true ancestors of humanity, and thus true children could not be born. Without true children, this world became the world of Satan. Therefore, this must be restored. That is why we established Parents' Day, Children's Day, and All Things Day in the First 7-Year Course. 
The reason is that Adam and Eve fell at the completion stage of their growth and could not become true parents, losing their children, all things, and even God, so this must be restored. Thus, the period of laying the foundation for restoring what was lost is the 1960s. Also, having become evil ancestors, good ancestors must emerge again. This standard was established in the 1960s. 
Now is the time when Adam and Eve are approaching God as children. That is, Adam and Eve, who are going through the growth process of rebirth, growth, and completion, are now establishing a relationship with God as true children who have not fallen. Therefore, this era is the era of children. Then what is the era of parents? The era of parents is the era of completion. 
Since the 7-Year Course started in 1960, we must enter the completion stage of the completion level. Since we must go through the number 7 in the first stage, it becomes 21, that is, 21 years up to the third stage. 
That is why the First 7-Year Course has completed the period of rebirth. Thus, we can go through the growth stage and head towards the completion stage. 
Jacob completed the internal foundation to move towards a new nation after 21 years. 
After proclaiming Parents' Day in 1960, we completely subdued Satan during the 7-year period. This is because we must return to the position of Adam and Eve before the fall. 
Fallen parents are parents who were fallen by Satan, so they can be invaded by Satan. Therefore, they lost all of Parents' Day, Children's Day, and All Things Day. That is why we have restored Parents' Day, Children's Day, and All Things Day. In this position, we established Parents' Day, Children's Day, and All Things Day centered around parents, going through the 7-year process. 
By going through this, we have restored the children lost in the world of Satan, restored families, restored tribes, and established conditions for the indemnity restoration of nations. This is the standard that Jesus should have found centered on Judaism and Israel. 
In the First 7-Year Course, we established Parents' Day, Children's Day, and All Things Day, and finally, on January 1, 1968, we could establish God's Day. 
By finding all the conditions lost due to the fall of parents, we are now at the time to establish the individual, family, tribal, and national foundations for a national start. Therefore, being on this standard means that Adam and Eve have returned to the stage where they can be blessed. 
God wants to indemnify centered on nations and states. However, since the world of Satan has already formed nations, Jesus was sent to break them down. 
Since we have broken the conditions under which Satan could accuse us in the 7-Year Course, we have now been placed in a position where Satan cannot move. Now that everything that needs to be indemnified has been indemnified, it is the time when Satan and we can become brothers. No one can disregard us carelessly. It took 21 years to prepare this foundation. 
The position of the Unification Church
The standard we have restored until now is the basis on which Adam and Eve could start as true ancestors of humanity without falling in the Garden of Eden. Now is the time to prepare the forms of lost children, tribes, and nations. In that sense, we have laid down the conditions for indemnity centered on the nation. Now those conditions have been established. Therefore, until now, Cain has always been in a position to strike Abel, but from now on, we will enter a time of restoration where we can be welcomed. Of course, in the past, the Teacher has also been beaten a lot, but now everything has been regained. 
So what position is this era in? Originally, if humans had not fallen, they would have been in a position where God, Adam, and the archangel were one centered on God. However, due to the fall, they could not stand in that unified position. Therefore, we must establish a standard like that of Adam and Eve on earth to find the lost earth and spirit world. The spirit world, which has many spirits that have come and gone until now, is equivalent to the angelic world of the time of Adam. 
So what position does the Unification Church hold before God today? It is in the position of the descendants of Adam. Since we have passed the national and tribal indemnity hurdles centered on this lineage, we are now in an equal position. It is no longer the time when Cain struck Abel, but it has become a time when Esau welcomes Jacob. The time has come for the world to intersect in this connection. Since the earth has reached this time, the spirit world can cooperate with the earth. The spirit world, which is equivalent to the angelic world, has not been able to cooperate with the earth until now. This is because the fallen angels, that is, Satan, have been paired with humans. 
Now, centered on God, we have completed the original standard of completion, that is, the standard of original parents and children. Since Satan also knows the way of restoration, it is now time for him to retreat. Therefore, the spirit world, which has replaced the angelic world, must expel Satan from the position he occupied. 
Today, our Unification Church is in the position of Adam and Eve before the fall. Therefore, the angelic world must serve us. In other words, if Adam and Eve are to suffer, the angels must protect them. 
Today, the Unification Church is in the position of Adam and Eve before the fall, so the spirit world, equivalent to the angelic world, must serve the Unification Church and obey absolutely. Now that the path has opened for Satan to be subdued and defeated, when Satan appears on the precious path we are taking, the spirit world, which is the angelic world, can be mobilized to strike Satan. Such battles are currently taking place in the spirit world. Spirits are fighting for the Unification Church. In other words, the time has come for spirits to take responsibility for Satan. Thus, they must fulfill the mission of unfallen angels in the spirit world. 
That is why we designated January 1, 1968, as God's Day and set the slogan for 1968 as "Let us make a full-scale advance." 
Indemnifying 6,000 years of history through the 7-Year Course
Now that we have established authority as parents, authority as children, and authority as all things, and authority as God, we must stop Satan's offensive. Until now, we have been driven by Satan, but now is the time when we can take the offensive in reverse. That is why we can set the slogan "Let us make a full-scale advance." 
This July is the month that surpasses the number 7. Just as Adam and Eve had to go through the process of the number 7, this month is the month that surpasses the number 7. 
When viewed centered on God, Adam and Eve are in the position of children, and God is in the position of a father. When viewed centered on the Teacher, the Teacher is in the position of parents, and everyone else is in the position of children. 
The seven months from January to July correspond to the period of restoring the fortune of 7,000 years in the 7-Year Course. Once we surpass this period, a new era will unfold. Therefore, spending the 40-day summer evangelistic period during this time has a heavenly significance. 
Up to the completion stage of the growth level, Adam and Eve are walking the path as children. They must rise to the completion level to become parents. 
Then what position are you in now? Your current position is like the position where Jesus was trying to make a new start centered on Judaism and the Israelite nation. Also, this position is like the position where Judaism should support Jesus, and the tribe and nation must unite to start. This position is like the form of restoring the fallen Adam's family by fulfilling the mission of children. You must go through 7 years from here. At the starting point, it is the standard of children, but by going through this process, you will become parents. 
Originally, centered on children, you must go through this process in unity with Korea, Christianity, and the Teacher's family. It must be as Jesus intended centered on Judaism and the Israelite nation. If you do this for just 7 years, it would be easy, but because unity could not be achieved, it took 21 years. 
The Teacher's inability to establish a direct relationship with Korean Christianity is a resentment. Because he could not directly establish a connection with the 6,000 years of historical providence, the Teacher walked for 21 years centered on other lineages, leaving a resentment of not being able to connect with the direct lineage. 
During the 7-Year Course, we have laid the foundation for individual restoration, tribal restoration, and national restoration, but the foundation of the 6,000 years of providence still remains. This must be indemnified, but who will do this? Today, the Unification Church is moving forward from a position that corresponds to the children’s generation, which is one step below the Teacher. Therefore, now you must walk the 7-Year Course and indemnify and restore the 6,000 years of history. The Second 7-Year Course is whose time? It is your time, the Unificationists. 
The resentment of Jesus is that the tribe and the Jewish denomination and the Israelite nation could not become one. Even until he was crucified, Jesus could not connect that standard. Therefore, God's achievements until now have been inherited by the person who has worked the hardest. 
When looking at denominations, our church is Abel, and the established churches are Cain. However, to completely restore the parents, we cannot restore with just Abel. Cain and Abel must unite to serve the parents for the parents to be restored. In that sense, the Unification Church, which is an Abel-like denomination, and the established churches must unite. The time has come when we can cooperate with each other to completely subdue Satan. Therefore, we are conducting an interdenominational movement to establish the condition of Cain and Abel becoming one. You must understand this content to know how indemnity restoration takes place. 
Even when looking at nations, democracy and communism correspond to Abel and Cain. This must also be achieved through the victory alliance. 
Therefore, the Teacher has established the conditions for indemnity for world restoration. Since the Teacher has come to this earth and established such conditions and has risen to the position of parents, he cannot go down again. Now it is the turn of the children. Therefore, the children must resolve the Teacher's resentment. 
Then what position are you in now? You are in the position of having taken over the nation of Israel that God prepared for 4,000 years, the position of having inherited the Jewish denomination that Jesus was trying to entrust, and the position of having taken all the conditions given to Joseph's family. Not only that, but the blessed families are in the position of having received the place of the bride and groom that Jesus was seeking while being chased and oppressed. 
Because you are in such an incredible position, you are being persecuted both inside and outside. 
We are in a position that transcends the place of the Lamb's Feast that the deceased Jesus must achieve after 2,000 years of effort. Being in such a position means that we are not in a position of having lost the church, nation, and tribe, but rather in a position where we can find them. Therefore, at this time, we are told to become the national messiahs for the blessed families. 
Being blessed means that the messiah has laid the foundation on earth through 2,000 years of effort, and it is now time to start in the name of the bride and groom centered on the chosen nation, denomination, and tribe. You can become the tribal messiahs.
Is it? Because the connection between the teacher and the father-son relationship has been established, even Satan cannot move. Blessings are truly immense. 

However, this does not mean that you are better than Jesus and the Holy Spirit. Since we are resolving the grief of the restoration of the tribe, Jesus should also be grateful. 

So what should we do at this time? Of course, we should follow the path that the teacher walked, and we must indemnify the path that Jesus took. And we must not forget to find the eight members of Noah's family. 

Even if we evangelized during the first seven-year course, it means that we evangelized in support of the teacher's course. Therefore, the children of faith that you evangelized become the teacher's children. Thus, you do not have to take responsibility for them. However, from now on, those who evangelize will become the center of the father-son relationship, so if you leave the children you connected during the 40-day summer evangelism period in the second seven-year course, it will be a big problem. 

If you do not guide and raise the children of faith you evangelized well during the second seven-year course, later, even if they accuse you, you will not be able to move. This is especially true for blessed families. This is because it is the same as abandoning children born within one's own tribal realm and making them orphans. If these orphans grab their parents by the collar and demand responsibility, there will be no way to respond. 

Therefore, during this evangelism period, those who evangelized must nurture and raise them. Whether through letters or material connections, you must ensure that they can treat you like parents. If you fail to do so, the problem will become difficult. It will be like the countless humans who have been unable to move even after accusing Adam and Eve for 6,000 years. Therefore, by fulfilling each of your responsibilities, the teacher's grief will be resolved. 

Now our time is coming. Even if they try to persecute and eliminate us, they cannot. We must confidently advance with the rightful heavenly authority. Those who are not blessed must find and establish the three children of faith to form families, and blessed families must stand in a position like Noah's eight members centered around the teacher's family. 

In going through the world restoration course, God's family must expand tribally centered on the three families of the teacher's children of faith. 

We must find and establish the 12 sons of Jacob and the 70 families, as well as the 12 elders of Moses' 12 tribes. The teacher established these conditions starting from the 1960s. Therefore, in order for you to stand in the position of tribal messiah, you must establish these conditions. 

Blessed families must establish the son-in-law expectation centered on the teacher's family. In this way, the family that is established is the family that Adam was originally supposed to establish. If this does not happen, one cannot start with the will of Jesus as a tribal messiah. A family that has established the son-in-law expectation centered on God will form 12 families when it radiates outward. 

When viewed centered on Jesus, the three disciples must receive blessings and establish the son-in-law expectation. Then it becomes eight members, which will replace Adam or Noah's eight members. However, Jesus could not fulfill his will. Without receiving blessings, one cannot become a child of heaven. 

When the teacher's family and your triune family become one centered on God, all conditions for Satan's accusations will be cut off, and from the position of tribal messiah, we can advance toward the world. Thus, the son-in-law expectation must be established, and the eight members must become one. 

The reason Jesus urged the three disciples not to fall asleep three times in the Garden of Gethsemane was to walk the path of a shared destiny as sons. However, they did not understand Jesus' deep intention and were just sleeping. Therefore, Jesus found himself in the same position as having lost family members in the Adam family. Consequently, he could not restore the substantial Cain and Abel, nor could he become the Messiah who could restore the substance. Here, Jesus could not avoid death, and God could not help but establish Jesus again from a spiritual standpoint and start anew. 

To align with God's purpose and direction, if the three disciples had completely united with Jesus and had three children of faith, then there would be 12 disciples united with Jesus. These disciples are representatives to indemnify historical sins. 

We must restore the three sons in the position of Cain. Who is in the position of Cain? It is the archangel. Because the archangel fell during the time of Adam, the result was the loss of three angels. This must be restored through three generations. 

The three disciples of Jesus must serve with a heart of obedience and submission from the time Jesus' direct children were in the womb, just as the three angels cooperated when God created Adam. If they do not do this, they cannot establish that standard. Once that standard is established, the three angels will be liberated in the spirit world. Therefore, the three children of faith are absolutely necessary. When that happens, the 12 disciples become one before Jesus. 

When we look at God's work, Peter is the restorative form of fallen Adam, James is the form of Jesus, and John the Apostle is the form of the returning Lord. In the age of the returning Lord, he must govern the earth centered on love, so John the Apostle is the apostle of love. Therefore, the apostle John, who symbolizes the returning Lord, must not die. Thus, while the other disciples died on the cross, John the Apostle did not die on the cross. Peter, being in the form of Adam, was crucified upside down and died. 

Blessed families are in the position of having established the son-in-law expectation centered on the teacher's family, but this alone cannot organize the tribes. Only by filling the 12 numbers can we finally enter a new stage of tribal restoration. Therefore, blessed families must find and establish the children of faith to create the 12 tribes. Failing to do this was the grief of Jesus. However, by fulfilling this, we can start as a new tribal messiah. 

Then, what should be the emotional standard of the children of faith? It must be a standard that can replace parents even in the position of death, in contrast to the disciples who betrayed Jesus on the cross. If that happens, these children of faith will stand in the position representing the historical form of Cain. However, if they cannot absolutely serve Abel from the position representing Cain, the conditions of grief and the conditions for Satan's accusations will remain. Therefore, the children of faith must be in a position to serve Abel with obedience and submission from the time the direct children of their parents are in the womb. Only then can they indemnify the conditions that even the angels could not fulfill. 

If they fail to do this, the conditions for Satan's accusations will remain. 

The teacher and you have been working hard together since 1960 to lay this foundation, eating barley rice and enduring hardships. Therefore, the teacher set the slogan for the first year of the seven-year course to be "Make this the year with the greatest achievements in life." Thus, in that long-awaited year in history, we finally found families, and the slogan for the following year was set to "Become the representative of God." 

This meant to take on the mission in place of the father centered on the children. When we have a position that can show and boast about this foundation, family victory becomes easy. Thus, the latter four years were set to be a time to become victorious subjects. We just need to connect this. 

We cannot fathom how great a blessing it is to participate in this seven-year course. One thing to know is that your ancestors have had no merit in the providence of restoration until now. When have the families blessed through the teacher ever cooperated to bear fruit like Abraham, Noah, or Moses? It is because the teacher blessed you that you have borne fruit. 

The fact that you have borne fruit is similar to how the Messiah Jesus appeared as the fruit of 4,000 years of history. Moreover, since you are the culmination of 6,000 years of history, it would be a great problem if you cannot conclude all connections and conditions. 

Because you are blessed, your ancestors can also start within the benefits of victory. Thus, the time will come when your ancestors can freely return to the earth and cooperate. Now is the time when you can liberate your ancestors from the 70th generation or even over 200 generations. You must understand that without such connections, the end times cannot appear. Now we have entered the era of the providence of restoration. 

The second seven-year course is the time when the teacher's seven-year course is completely finished and the foundation is laid, and for you, it is the time when all victories and defeats are determined. 

The teacher is the first generation, and you are the second generation. You, as the second generation, must completely occupy the fortune of Korea during this seven-year course. You must know this and walk the seven-year course. The path you must take is not even one-hundredth of the path the teacher walked. You do not face the same persecution or opposition that the teacher faced. 

What you should be even more grateful for is that the teacher has not yet conveyed the words to his physical parents and siblings, but now that the foundation for tribal restoration has been prepared, you can weep and convey the words centered on your own tribe. In the past, the firstborn restoration was done by establishing the second born, but that era ends with the teacher. However, since you are in a position that has the authority of the firstborn restoration, older brothers must bring their younger siblings out, even if they have to hit them. Based on that foundation, even if you organize your tribe, Satan cannot accuse you. 

People must have a purpose, and there must be a clear direction toward that purpose. Thus, through that direction, they must solve their life problems. 

Now, God's purpose and direction is for you to organize the 12 tribes. Just as Jesus came to this earth to organize the 12 tribes and attempt a global start, it is the same for us today. The organization of the 12 tribes, which is God's purpose and direction, must become the center of our lives in reality. Only those who can achieve this can align with God's purpose and direction and live in the kingdom of heaven. This is the core of the providence of restoration. 

What should we do in the second seven-year course? We must become true sons and daughters of God by carrying out the tasks pointed out earlier, just like Jesus. 

Let us tighten our belts once again and run vigorously to make these irreplaceable days in a precious era that cannot return! 

**The Significance of the Second Seven-Year Course and the Responsibility of Children**
<Summary of the Words> The second seven-year course is the course that the members must take. The question was how to lead them according to the original intention of the early days. The significance of the recent regional leader changes lies here. 

The results of the teacher's nationwide tour this time were generally reassuring. If we consider a person's life to be 70 years, and subtract the nights, there are only 35 years left. Furthermore, if we exclude the time spent on basic necessities, the actual time spent living is very little. How many people live each day feeling true happiness for even an average of 30 minutes that the universe would envy? 

We are in a position where we cannot even have 10 minutes of comfort or joy in a day. The struggle of the heart and body has sown seeds that have borne fruit today in the democratic world (the world of the heart) and the communist world (the physical world). 

No matter how insignificant a creature may be, there is God's sincerity in it. It was not created haphazardly. The purpose of creating it was to rejoice and to live together. 

God's greatest masterpiece is humanity. This is undeniable even when observing the intricate structure of the human body. 

Humans are not poorly created; they are ultimately flawed. Humans are unfinished products. That is why they desire to be complete. 

If humans were complete, how would God have treated them? He would have placed them in the highest position and loved them. That position is where the father-son relationship is established. To become God's sons and daughters, one must completely occupy God's love to find complete peace. In the world, one loves as the subject, but to occupy God's love, one must become the motivation for others to become the subject. 

Public - eternal, centered on the whole 
Private - temporary, centered on the self 
Let us not become those who give and seek a return. Pray that what you seek may be granted even after tens of thousands of years. The ideals of such people continue for tens of thousands of years. If you do not shed tears thinking of the teacher, it is fake. Do not remember the help you give to others. 

You must silently dedicate your life for your parents. You must do the same for your siblings. 

The teacher has walked this path for decades but has not yet grown weary. There is no time to be tired. When I was in Chuncheon, Yoon Cheongjeong sent a telegram saying that the world of resentment has passed and the world of glory has returned. 

Giving is about giving your own. I must become the greatest low-pressure zone. 

Because God is eternal, humans, as His children, must also be eternal. To be good and eternal, one must become an unchanging person. 

Conscience does not tire; it becomes more sensitive. 

Those who watch fights are evil, and those who try to stop fights are good. God also created religion to stop human fights. After stopping the fights, regeneration must occur. That regeneration factory is religion. Everyone must go through the regeneration factory. The better and more capable a person is, the more they need religion. 

Hell is a warehouse for broken souls. Even if you die, you must not go to hell. To avoid death, you must enter the regeneration factory. Jesus is the technical manager of the regeneration factory. 

Heaven is the warehouse for completed products. 

Religion teaches about God. Religion comes from God. Therefore, religion must have the power to govern human life and death. 

The world is filled with parts factories. Now there must be a factory that integrates them. That is the Unification Church. Its owner is the returning Lord. 

And religion must heal diseases. 

All diseases must be healed. 

If both sides are similar in strength, they will fight. If the difference in strength is large, there will be no fight. 

They are sincere. A sincere parent knows the misfortunes of a child who is away. If one is sincere, they will communicate. Practice asceticism. 

You must cut down the 6,000-year-old wild olive tree and graft in the seedling of the true olive tree. In other words, you must cut off the trunk of the old tree and graft in a new seedling. 

Adam is the masculine God in substance, and Eve is the feminine God in substance. 

Evil beings cannot eternally dominate good. 

Jesus, being the latter Adam, was supposed to meet the latter Eve and hold a holy wedding, but because he could not, he drove another nail into God's heart. 

The returning Lord is the third Adam. The returning Lord must resolve the grievances from two occasions. 

The Unification Church aims to resolve and achieve all grievances created by the failures of Adam and Jesus. 

The reason Jesus could not fulfill his will lies in the first responsibility of the Joseph family and the second responsibility of John the Baptist. 

Christianity was not established through the principle of the cross but through the principle of resurrection. 

Humans come into the world with the ability to see light and perceive all things even before they are born. There must be a cause that gives purpose to the eyes. 

If you receive a gift incorrectly, you will be caught by heavenly law. 

The year 1960 corresponds to the completion stage of growth. The completion period is seven years.
In 1960, three children were established at the completion level of the Changseong period. These three children symbolize Peter, John, and James. By finding the Adam family, the restoration of the spirit and physical world married in the world of Satan becomes possible. The 36 families represent the restoration type of the ancestors of humanity. The 72 families represent the restoration of Cain and Abel (restoration of children). The 124 families represent the nations of the world. (Among them, four established families are included.) Based on that foundation, the selection of holy sites was made, which amounts to 120 holy sites in 40 countries worldwide. By proclaiming God's Day on January 1, 1968, the position of unfallen parents was restored. As a result, Satan was completely removed, and humanity was fully restored. This year marked the beginning of a full-scale advance. The period from January to July of this year corresponds to 7,000 years of history.

**The Second Seven-Year Course and the Responsibility of Children**
The first seven-year course is the era of the restoration of the Cain and Abel brothers, but the second seven-year course is the era of the restoration of children. Today's second seven-year course is in the same position as when the teacher started the seven-year course right after liberation. However, unlike then, we are welcomed rather than persecuted. One must restore even younger siblings by any means necessary, akin to how Cain killed his younger brother Abel. Young men and women must restore the three children of faith. Then, together with the parents of faith, they will restore a family of eight. They must create children who can die in their place. The three children of faith represent the restoration type of the three archangels. Just as the three archangels supported and cooperated with Adam and Eve from the time of creation, the children of faith must carry and raise the blessed children of their parents of faith from the womb until they are married, in order to establish the standard for their own restoration. Without being blessed and giving birth to sons and daughters, one cannot enter the kingdom of heaven. The newly evangelized children of faith must not be left alone. That would be like giving birth to a child and abandoning it on the street. They must be led for seven years.

1. Existence in place of Adam… Seven-year course

For a Unification Church member, the most terrifying words are to not go through the seven-year course and to not engage in 40 days of activity.

**Restoration of Families and the World**
Genesis 1:27-31
**Prayer (I)** Father, today is the first day of September 1968, the day we finish the 100-day prayer period and the 40-day activity period. The children who were scattered during that time have gathered here in the main sanctuary, so Father, please look upon them with a heart of compassion. 
Gracious Father, we know that you have gathered us not to seek anything in this world, but to achieve the overall purpose you have longed for and to establish a victorious good nation on this earth. 
Father, we have a longing for the true form of children who would have been exceedingly good, glorious, and lovely if humanity's ancestors had not fallen in the original world. Therefore, please allow us to pursue that good place of our ancestors that they could not occupy, a nation where we can be eternally protected in your love and live forever with your eternal love. We are well aware of how much you have labored since that day, as our ancestors made mistakes and lost the original standard you established. 
Father, we know that your sorrowful tears shed on the path of restoration permeate the historical process of humanity and our current living environment. Please let us clearly understand that we have the duty and responsibility as your sons to remove the sad facts of history and to eliminate all the sad circumstances of your heart in reality. 
Father, we know that this year, 1968, is indeed a significant year. This year marks the end of the first seven-year course and the beginning of the second seven-year course, as we have decided to march toward the battlefield. We have already sworn to dedicate our lives for the day of your desire. Therefore, we have the determination to follow your will until we establish a nation of your victory, whether we live or die, so please allow us to become your sons and daughters who can die for your will and live for your will. We earnestly hope and wish for this. 
Father, we know that we have the responsibility to shed blood and sweat for this nation and this people, and for all of humanity. We understand that we must fight until everything returns to heaven, and we earnestly hope and wish that you will make us victors in all battles as we fulfill our respective responsibilities. 
Your children, who were scattered in the mountains and fields, have gathered here today, so Father, please embrace them and comfort them. Are there any of your children who are wounded? Please comfort them. Are there any children who have resolved to follow your will in this new relationship? Please let the flag of heavenly life that surges in their hearts move forward. May this time be one where they lament their own suffering in the world of death, express gratitude for their newfound liberation, and give glory to you, Father. 
Today is a holy day. We know that many of your children scattered throughout South Korea have gathered to worship before you on this day, so please embrace them with uniform grace and govern their hearts and bodies with the grace of life. Thus, we earnestly hope and wish that you will make them your faithful soldiers who can achieve your desired purpose and your wishes. 
Today, your children scattered around the world are longing for this headquarters with tearful hearts, hoping to meet again, so we earnestly hope and wish that you will comfort them. Also, there are your sons who hold onto the mission you have given and bear the mission of pioneers in lonely places abroad, so please be with them wherever they are. May you testify that you are alive and establish a foundation for your victory by manifesting your authority in that environment. 
Please allow all that they desire to be fulfilled throughout the world, and since our purpose in fighting is not only for this nation and this people but also to restore the entire world, may we resolve again, unite again, and pledge again to become your sons and daughters who can make progress in front of your will until the day of victory. 
Now, we wish to dedicate this hour to you, Father, so please oversee everything. Do not let it be a time where Satan can intrude. Please let our hearts be solely captivated by you. May this time be one where we remove the root of sin and, as true beings who can only be governed by you, bow before you. 
We earnestly ask that you personally oversee everything, and we offer all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen. 
**Prayer (II)** Father, please embrace the children gathered here as your rightful children. They are the descendants who have made you lonely and sad throughout the long historical process. We know that the motivation and purpose for which you have labored is for your children, so please grant us the connection to embrace them as your beloved children at this time, Father. 
We know that no one can step forward to ask for blessings or to plead for blessings before you. However, through your infinite mercy, love, and labor, you have allowed us to have the connection to become your sons and daughters, and through that connection, we can call upon your name. 
We must inherit your highness, your preciousness, and your power. Therefore, we realize once again that we must fulfill the overall mission of subduing the remaining enemies throughout the universe, and we hope that this time will be one where we pledge to carry out that mission. 
We are but naked and insufficient beings who have nothing. We should be the ones to apologize a thousand or ten thousand times whenever we bow before your presence. Yet, despite this, you have become the sacrificial offering in our place until now, abandoning the foundation of glory, and have labored through suffering and adversity to open the path for humanity. We earnestly hope and wish that we will clearly understand that you are such a Father. 
We must become your children who can truly call you Father with hearts that are connected to you. How much must we long for you, Father? Yet, we, who have carried the grievance of losing you for 6,000 years, how much do you long for us to break through that grievance and call out to you as our Father, embracing us in your arms and weeping? We understand your heart well, Father. Therefore, we earnestly hope and wish that we can become your sons and daughters. 
Father, this time, your children have gathered here again after going through various trials during the 40-day course of pioneers. All the facts we have overcome in that difficult journey were because we loved heaven, and we have come here with a heart that loves you more. Therefore, please stretch out your hands of compassion and mercy at this place, and remember them deeply in your heart. Please cover them with your profound love and grant them the strength and courage to reach the eternal foundation of happiness. 
Father, we know that there are children here who are attending for the first time. We know that anyone can surely be your child belonging to heaven, so please embrace them. May this hour allow our hearts and bodies to unite and affirm that we are your bloodline, giving us a new resolution and determination. Thus, may we be your sons and daughters who take on the responsibility of standing with heaven on behalf of this nation and this world and walk the path of battle against the world of enemies. 
We dedicate this hour before you, Father, so please personally oversee everything. We wish to convey your words in this short time, so please let the hearts of the speaker and the listener become one. May you be the center of all the words and bring about a new transformation in our hearts, completely severing the bitter roots of sin. Thus, may you alone govern everything and create an atmosphere where only you can preside over everything, manifesting your authority, your life, and your power here. 
Please do not let this be a time where we are mocked by enemies, but rather let it be a time where we can experience your deep and high love and the grace of life under your power and protection. 
Please remember your children scattered throughout South Korea who are longing for this place, and also remember those scattered around the world who are fighting centered on your will in loneliness. We know that their tears and sweat are all because they love you, so please be with them, and discern their paths, allowing them to establish a foundation for victory that can be gathered toward heaven. 
Today is the first day of a new month and the first Sunday, so we earnestly hope and wish for your blessings upon this day. Two-thirds of this year has passed, and one-third remains. Now, centered on these remaining days, we have the task of achieving the goal of our declared slogan of full-scale advance this year, so please personally work with us in the process of achieving that, allowing us to establish a standard to boast of our decisive victory centered on this nation and this people. 
At this time, we earnestly ask that you allow us to share your words with your children solely within your will, and we offer all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen. 
**Message** The title of today's message is "Restoration of Families and the World." 
**Heaven's Providence to Find One Person**
Human beings living on this earth were originally meant to be the good sons and daughters of God. However, we know that they could not become the good lineage of heaven and were born as descendants of the opposing position. It is often said that this world is an evil world, regardless of who you ask. This means that it has not become a good world but has turned into an evil one. Consequently, even those living in this evil world cannot help but become evil people. In other words, today’s humanity lives from the standpoint of good and its opposite. 
Originally, when humanity was to start on this earth, if they had begun with God at the center as good ancestors, we would not have to seek a new world or pursue a new ideal in this historical process today. However, due to the fall of humanity's ancestors, we have become obligated to seek a new nation of hope and a new world of hope. 
If humanity's ancestors had not fallen, what kind of world would it have been? If they had formed families centered on the eternal heart and love of God as God's lineage, then tribes would have formed around those families, and nations and the world would have automatically been established centered on those tribes. That world would undoubtedly have been one that could receive God's dominion under God's sovereignty. However, the fact that the world became the opposite of that is the retribution and result of the fall. Thus, God has not been able to directly govern the countless humans living on this earth but has been pushing forward the history of providence from an indirect position, needing to save these humans. This is what we know as the history of religion until now. 
Since the fallen descendants of Adam and Eve were born, fallen families, fallen religions, fallen nations, and a fallen world have been established on this earth. God must find one person in this fallen world, the world of enemies, but it is impossible to find a person whom God can love from a natural standpoint. To find a person that God can use and establish in this world of enemies, the history of struggle must be repeated. To find that one person, God must take the lead in pioneering the environment and reveal God's internal situation. Thus, one individual...
bear in a way that is more profound than those who came before. This is the path that must be followed to return to the original world.

In conclusion, the history of humanity has been a journey of restoration, a return to the original state that was lost due to the fall. The mission of Jesus, who is to return, is to establish a new nation on this earth and conquer the world of evil. This is the purpose of the returning Messiah, who must continue the work that was started 2,000 years ago. 

The world today, despite being shaped by democracy and the legacy of Israel, lacks the true individuals, families, tribes, nations, and states that can represent God's heart and fulfill His will. The restoration process is ongoing, and it is essential for humanity to seek the path back to the original world, where God can truly dwell among His people. 

The ultimate goal is to create a world where God can be the eternal parent, where love can flourish, and where humanity can live in harmony with the divine. This is the world we must strive to return to, and it is through the restoration of our original nature that we can achieve this.
A responsible leader who is more thorough than the ancestors of humanity must emerge. This leader should not be someone who betrays heaven for their own glory and desires, but rather a central being who can forsake all their desires and even sacrifice their life for the will of heaven. To establish such a being, heaven has been working throughout history. Thus, the one sent as such a representative is Jesus. Therefore, Jesus is different from Adam and Eve. 

Adam and Eve fell from the desire to rise higher due to their enlightened eyes, but Jesus did not betray God even in the face of death. He prayed three times in the Garden of Gethsemane, worrying about God's will. "Abba, Father, all things are possible for You; take this cup away from Me; nevertheless, not what I will, but what You will." (Mark 14:36). This prayer was not of human will but was the beginning of Jesus’ alignment with the Father’s will, and this was indeed the path of Jesus’ death. There, Jesus established a standard that surpassed the fallen ancestors of humanity. 

Jesus had to love and honor God more than Adam did. He also had to hate Satan, whom God despises, more than anyone else. Therefore, He had to inherit the foundation of victory that God had prepared throughout the historical process without any shortcomings. In other words, He had to eliminate the conditions for Satan's accusations that existed in the historical process. Furthermore, in terms of the era, centered on the nation of Israel, He had to possess the authority to remove any conditions that could lead to the accusations of Satan due to the mistakes of the Israelite people. He had to stand in a position that could completely replace the original standard that Satan could not invade. Additionally, Jesus had to be in emotional unity with God and stand on an absolute standard centered on God’s hope. In every aspect, Jesus had to be superior to Adam and Eve. Without this, He could not be the Savior. 

After 4,000 years, the son who was finally placed in such a position, centered on Judaism and established as a seed in the household of Joseph, was Jesus. At that time, since the side of Satan was forming a nation to attack heaven, there had to be a national standard of a complete foundation on heaven's side as well. Thus, God worked for 4,000 years to establish one nation. The merit of God's hard work was that through the Israelite people accepting Jesus, it became a global foundation, and a world centered on God and Jesus had to be established on this earth. However, because Jesus died, that world was only realized spiritually. 

What should be done about this spiritual Israel? Today, Christianity is not like the ancient nation of Israel. Among the Christian nations of the world, there are many individuals, families, tribes, and nations who say, "Lord, come to our country," but there is no country that can assert that Jesus will definitely come to their nation. There is no nation that has become like the nation of Israel when Jesus came 2,000 years ago. 

Our nation has laid the foundation to welcome the Lord for thousands of years. There is no country that can assert that the Lord will definitely come among our people and within our nation. There is nothing sadder than a nation without a homeland, yet that is how it has become. 

Today, Christians think, "Ah, the Lord must come on the clouds." How wonderful would that be? If that were truly the case, people like us wouldn’t have to suffer. If they believed that way, they would have believed enough not to lose to pastors and elders. They would have been as diligent as anyone else in their devotion. What would the Lord do if He came on the clouds? 

If we dissect the history of Christianity, it has only emerged spiritually, suffering and being slaughtered. Because there was no foundation on the earth, they had to be slaughtered and sacrificed by numerous sovereigns of nations. Just that alone is frustrating and resentful, and what would the Lord do if He were to come spiritually as the returning Lord? Would He take away the Christians and kill everyone else? God is certainly not that kind of being. Like the parable of the prodigal son, we must understand that God is a God who loves the prodigal son more than His eldest son. 

What would the Lord do if He came to this earth and judged all people, creating a sea of death and turning them to ashes, fulfilling God's will? Judgment is not about judging people; it is about judging the enemy, Satan. 

The Bible says that if someone sins, they should be forgiven seventy times seven. Why must we continue to forgive those who have sinned? Does it mean that after forgiving them, we will kill them all later? No. People must be forgiven and saved, but Satan cannot be treated that way. People can be forgiven, but the devil cannot. Repeated forgiveness is a strategy to expel the enemy. Do you understand what I mean? Because these enemies have tormented humanity, forgiving them is a strategy for revenge against the enemy. 

What is the overall purpose of the restoration providence? Among the 3 billion people in the world today, how many are Christians? These Christians all claim that when the Lord comes, they must participate in the first resurrection, but is the first resurrection that easy? How can they resurrect without knowing that? What percentage of them will be resurrected? Will they leave only those people behind and strike down all of humanity? Such a delusional faith cannot be accepted. We must save the earth. We must save the earth. To do that, we must first completely save individuals from the world of Satan on the earth. Families must also be completely saved on the earth. We must save the heavenly tribes, nations, and ultimately the country on the earth. It is not in the air; it must be on the earth. What was lost during the fall was not lost in the air but on the earth. 

Restoration means to find what was lost again. What was lost must be found in the place where it was lost. It was lost on the earth, so it must be reclaimed on the earth. 

A person who has a body and mind fell. Therefore, centered on people, we must completely deny Satan and stand in the position of Adam and Eve, who can receive God's love as sons and daughters. Such a person cannot be dominated by Satan. They dominate Satan. Satan was originally the archangel. The archangel is meant to be governed by humanity. We are recovering that standard. Thus, the problem is not that there is no church like the Christian church. Also, it is not a matter of how many or how few church members there are. Such things cannot be God's will. What must exist before the church? There must be families. And before families, individuals must be restored. Isn’t that how it should be? 

If the ancestors of humanity had originally not violated God's laws and had been united with God forever, no one could take them away in that united love connection. They were already born as sons and daughters, and after growing up, there would be no theory or doctrine that could deny their identity by explaining, "Hey, who is your father? Isn’t that your father?" Even if they were threatened with swords, it would not work. 

Today, humans are born from God but cannot act as His sons and daughters. The first reason is that God cannot love humans as His sons and daughters. God cannot love humanity, and humanity cannot receive love as God's sons and daughters. The second reason is that they cannot perform the sacrament as God's beloved sons and daughters, and the third is that they cannot establish a heavenly family centered on God's love. If they had achieved these three things, humanity would not have become as miserable as it is today. If that had happened, the cultural world we see today would have already been established long ago. However, because it did not happen, we have been tracing the path of restoration and are now talking about cultural worlds and whatnot. 

Therefore, we must find the place where we will ultimately meet, the place where we will ultimately stay. The nations of the world must find their original homeland, and countless humans must find their original hometown and parents. This is the ultimate purpose of God's providence so far. That is why today I am speaking about the restoration of families and the world. 

What will the Lord do when He comes? Christians say, "Oh, when the Lord comes to this world, He will bring judgment." They say everything will melt away. But where is such a nonsensical statement? Of course, it may be written in the Bible, but what will the Lord truly do when He comes? He must have authority to act against the sovereigns of the world. However, there is no such foundation on this earth. Will the Lord come to the fighting Christians and act? If He were to act in the spiritual realm, why would it take 6,000 years? If that were the case, why didn’t He just do it all in the Garden of Eden and multiply the clans? It does not work that way, as Christians believe. 

Even if He intends to judge the world, there must be a proper foundation. When God sent Jesus, He first created the nation of Israel centered on Jacob's family and Jacob's tribe. Then He sent Jesus to that nation. Therefore, the returning Lord must prepare to exercise judgment over the world. How can the Lord act when He comes to a spiritual nation like Christianity? 

So where must the Lord come? Will He come to any country within the Christian realm of democratic nations? He cannot come as a nation. He cannot come as a nation. Will He come to a place like America? Absolutely not. He cannot come there. If that were the case, I would not be doing this work. The Lord comes to meet individuals. How many people fell in the Garden of Eden? Two fell. Therefore, if the Lord comes as a man, who will He seek? He will seek a bride. What does the bride mean here? Today, all Christians around the world claim to be the bride of Jesus. Of course, from a relative standpoint, they may be brides, but that is indirect. 

Since the Lord comes as a man, He seeks to find conditions where He can fulfill the eternal ideal and establish a foundation for eternal happiness. He also seeks conditions that can fulfill the whole in establishing a heavenly family. Because the Lord comes with such content as a man, He seeks individuals on the ground who have such overall content and attitude. He seeks individuals, and since the Lord is male, He seeks females. He is looking for a bride. Because there is a standard of hope for the one bride, God has been laying the foundation for Christianity for 2,000 years. 

Unless individuals are found here, families cannot be found. Unless families are found, tribes cannot be found, and unless tribes are found, nations cannot be found. Without finding nations and tribes, we cannot think about restoring the world. That is why the Lord first seeks individuals. Do you understand? The Lord is not seeking Christianity; He is seeking individuals who can offer 100% obedience before the Lord who comes, standing closest to heaven even within Christianity. 

The bridegroom, the Lord, must receive the bride. So what will He do after establishing the bride? He must establish a family. People treat what I say as heretical, but we must see who is heretical and who is orthodox, who will perish and who will prosper. 

By receiving the bride, the returning Lord finally brings about the restoration of families. The family of restoration that must be found is the family that humanity hopes for. Throughout 6,000 years of history, many religious leaders who believed and came forth have been sacrificed by numerous rulers and politicians, and what they earnestly hoped for was that the Lord would come and repay their grievances and enemies. However, the Lord cannot repay their enemies alone. If He could have done it alone, He would have done it long ago. Therefore, a heavenly family must emerge. A heavenly family must be established to lay a new foundation on the earth. Thus, we must be able to explode the world of Satan with the dynamite of the heart. 

What is the purpose of God's creation? He did not create Adam and Eve just to look at them. He did not create man and woman for them to grow old and die. They were created so that as they grow up, through their mutual feelings towards each other, they could build a true paradise on earth centered on God. It was to create a foundation of love centered on God. Here, the male Adam represents heaven, and the female Eve represents the earth. Therefore, although they are two, when they unite horizontally, heaven and earth become one. When two people unite centered on God's love, the universe automatically unites. 

The reason Jesus has worked so hard to find the bride is for this reason. The two people who did not unite with God in the Garden of Eden and became servants due to their betrayal must completely unite for the origin of restoration to occur. What is that? It is the wedding feast of the Lamb. The Bible speaks of the wedding feast of the Lamb, which is the day when two people finally become one centered on God's love, the day when they are bound together, and that day is a day that all people have longed for, a day that can be celebrated throughout the ages. Thus, the purpose of providence, the history of humanity, and the purpose of religion all culminate there. 

Everyone here has families, but under whose protection is that family established? Some may think, "I live today in a way that is conscientious, and socially I am a person who will not lose to anyone." Therefore, they may feel confident and unashamed wherever they go. However, if we dig into the root, we find that the ancestors of humanity are caught in the snare of the enemy and cannot escape from that authority. Can a family established in such authority receive God's approval? That is why religions teach to live a single life. Even though many of you have had sons and daughters, you should have lived a single life. 

This is not just the words of Reverend Moon of the Unification Church. It is what religions teach. As you know, Buddhism teaches this too, and so does Catholicism. Do you know why? It is because they were taught that way as they drew closer to God. Those who were meant to be the true ancestors of humanity have not even had a wedding ceremony. Did they? No, they did not. Yet, can those who are in a position as if they have not been born have a wedding ceremony? The sons and daughters born as fallen descendants must all go through the hand of salvation to be restored.
We must walk the path. Originally, for us humans, things like religion, restoration, prayer, and any kind of return to God are all unnecessary. It should be that way. In the realm of God's love, it is possible to be that way. 

The two human ancestors, by separating from God, caused the tragic division of the heavenly lineage, ruining history. To restore this, the two must come together, and the day they unite will be the day of the Lamb's banquet. It is the day when Jesus returns to welcome the bride and hold the wedding feast of the bride and groom. That day was supposed to be when the true ancestor centered on God was to be born 6,000 years ago, but since that did not happen, it is only after 6,000 years that we can finally start toward the standard that God has desired, and humanity can return from the fallen world to the original world. 

Since the fall occurred on earth, restoration must also take place on earth. Then, since we speak of the family of restoration, who will be the center of that restored family? It must be a family made up of true sons and daughters whom God seeks, because that family is the purpose of God's creation. So, who will that be? It is the one who comes with the full authority to inherit the universe. That person is the Lord of the Second Advent. The Lord of the Second Advent must come and establish a family. If Christians hear this, they will be astonished. Jesus had to get married. If He didn't intend to get married, why would He have been born as a man? He would have been born as something neither male nor female. He would come as a being that is neither male nor female, acting as a woman when convenient and as a man when convenient. 

Today, there are many who swear by absurdities. The Lord will come on the clouds? What does that mean? When asked this, they say, "What do you mean? The Lord will do everything; I will just follow along." How ridiculous! They make their parents suffer and want everything for themselves. Think about it. Since the fall happened on earth, restoration must also happen on earth. If something is lost in the dirt, it must be found in the dirt; where is there a saying that something lost in the dirt can be found in the sky? This is nonsense. 

What is the wish of our Unification family? It is to become the family of restoration. Everyone, is that right? "Yes." I don't think so. (Laughter) Is that really true? "Yes." You must be able to believe it.... Our wish is here, the starting point of peace for all nations is here, the starting point of happiness in heaven and earth is here, the starting point of God's providence is here, the point of the great transformation of heaven and earth is here, the source of all human values is here, and the starting point of hope is here. It is all here. Then, who is the center of the family of restoration? It is the true ancestors. The true ancestors are the father and mother. 

Humans, due to the fall, can see their father and mother being reborn. Can you see fathers and mothers being born in the world? "No." Because of the fall, we can see that. It is a shocking fact. That is why Christianity teaches that one must be born again. It says one must enter the womb of the mother and be born again. But can one enter the womb of the mother again? No, so one must be grafted in. One must cut off the neck and graft in Jesus there. 

Today, many nations in the world are all brothers, yet they are fighting each other. Cain and Abel, who were brothers in Adam's family, fought and killed each other, and that brotherly fight has not yet ended. The history of wars in the world has been a continuation of brotherly fights. After the Second World War, brother nations entered a historical realm where they could be equal, so the victorious nations at that time liberated the defeated nations. Do you understand what I mean? It was time for the father and mother to come after the Second World War, so they said, "Now, let us not fight but reconcile and meet the father and mother together." It is reconciliation that allows us to meet the father and mother, isn't it? If we do not reconcile, when the father and mother come, everyone will be chased away, and both will perish, so we must reconcile. That was the Second World War. 

The history of humanity, which started with the fight of brothers, is now witnessing a conflict between the communist world and the democratic world. We must reconcile these. At this time, it is the Unification Church that must bring about this reconciliation. You may not believe it, but just wait and see. History has started from the war of brothers, and that fight has not yet been resolved. The victorious nations are like the elder brother, and the defeated nations are like the younger brother. Until now, the elder brother has beaten the younger brother to create history, but now it is time for the elder brother to liberate the younger brother. Thus, the war that took place to finally liberate the younger brother was the Second World War. Only then can the parents come and say, "Now these kids have become people; the old tendency to kill the younger brother has disappeared." The world has now entered a realm where it can welcome the parents. 

Since history has been the history of brotherly wars, who must come? The parents must come. However, until now, the parents have been born as fallen parents, contrary to the heavenly laws, so they have all been gathered among the children of enemies. It is all the opposite. Everything is opposite. As a result, the two fight. The two are always fighting, aren't they? Originally, they should not fight but should unite. The mind should represent heaven, and the body should represent the earth; also, the mind should represent the father, and the body should represent the mother, and they should have become one, but because they could not, everything became divided. God and humanity became separated. History began with the fight between Adam and Eve. It started with deception. 

It was said that if you eat, you will die. Yet, they thought, "Ah, it is okay to eat this. My eyes will be opened." It started with a deception that twisted the truth. From the very beginning, it was wrong. Therefore, we must suffer greatly based on that. We must pay the price for sin. We must reap what we have sown. 

At the end, the ties of brotherhood will all be severed. Until now, in human history, things like the heavenly way, the ties of parents and children, and the five relationships have been the foundation for managing this world, but at the end, all of those will break apart. When it becomes a time when mothers are what they are, children are what they are, wives are what they are, and husbands are what they are, you must understand that this is the end of the world. If it is said that parents stabbed their children with knives, that is the end, and if it is said that brothers stabbed each other, that is the end. When the world becomes a place where the uniqueness of brotherhood, the uniqueness of parent-child relationships, and the uniqueness of husband-wife relationships are all manipulated for self-centered purposes, that is the end. Because of the fall in the Garden of Eden, such things have been sown, and the time for the harvest of the fruits of the fall is coming. Isn't this the time? This world cannot just flow as it is; it has entered the harvest season, the time for reaping. 

The principle of restoration and the true parents' religion
The world has become what it is due to the fallen parents' ties that have deviated from God. Therefore, the true parents must come and establish a new ideology. What kind of ideology will that be? Will it be a world ideology? A heavenly ideology? It is the ideology of the true family. Without the ideology of the true family, the world ideology cannot emerge. The representative of this true family ideology must become the true son of God. He must be the internal heir who inherits all of God's emotional aspects, the external heir, and the heir of all things. In other words, he must be the one who can inherit God's heart, body, and all things. Only such a son can become God's representative. When that son comes, the kingdom of heaven will finally be established. 

So, what is the ideology of the true family? The ideology of the true family is the ideology of God's love. Isn't it simple? Without love, no matter how much one boasts of being the best in the world, that person is an unhappy person. Isn't that right? The ideology of the true family is one where when the parents go, the sons and daughters follow the parents forever, and when the elder brother goes, the younger brother follows forever, and when the younger brother goes, the elder brother follows forever. Therefore, if there is a nation of the younger brother, the nation of the elder brother must follow, and if there is a nation of the elder brother, the nation of the younger brother must also follow.
