Understanding God's internal affairs.

<Summary of the Message> Humanity lost God and creation due to the fall. Therefore, we must find what we have lost. How can we find parents, family, tribe, and nation? How can we meet our parents? What kind of person do we need to become to meet them? This is the problem.

There has been the hard work of those who have accompanied heaven. What you must understand is that by establishing this nation, you must inherit the historical labor of meeting God.

As you pass through the stages, the historical significance is applied to your internal feelings, making it increasingly difficult.

First, when restoring the family as an individual, family indemnity is necessary. Otherwise, you cannot align completely with the will. To transition to tribe, nation, and world, indemnity and sacrifice are essential. There must be spiritual, physical, and material sacrifices for national economic construction.

The entire history has worked hard to establish one person. There has been boundless historical effort to find one person, and today, establishing the Unification Church to restore families and tribes is the most pleasing thing to God.

You pass through the stages of ① family ② sons and daughters ③ relatives ④ nation.

You must come forward with explosive feelings. You cannot just stick to habitual thoughts. 

September 9, 1968, early morning, at the former headquarters church.
* This message was given during the early morning worship service and has been organized from the notes of the history compilation committee chairman, Yoo Kwang-ryeol. The title was added by the editor.

The history was disrupted because Abel of Adam's family and Ham of Noah's family made mistakes. You must not walk that path again; you must judge those mistakes and establish the standards of faithful sons and daughters. Unless you accept all historical mistakes as your own and repent and restore them, you cannot inherit the internal feelings that have been passed down historically.

God has walked a path of labor that cannot be completed even with a lifetime of repentance.
Humans are wicked. 
When the subject and object are reversed, they are under the control of Satan. We must serve God as the subject and stand in a relative position. However, humans try to place themselves as the subject and treat God as the object. 
Those who have come in and betrayed must not be neglected by those who come later. 
To become a member of the Unification Church, one must inherit God's and the Teacher's internal wishes. 
Parents should treat their sons and daughters as God treated and loved Adam and Eve. 
In what form and position will I meet God? Without inheriting this internal wish, tradition cannot be passed down. 
To meet God, one must know the historical path God has walked, understand the current circumstances, and know the standards of hope for the future. Otherwise, one cannot meet God. 
Establishing a family is not for personal well-being but to fight with a double cross. Therefore, tribes scatter to save their nations, and nations scatter again to seek other nations or the world. Blessed couples do not live well just for themselves. They must go. Even if they die, they must go while on the way, and even if they part, they must part while on the way. 
They must be absolutely intertwined with God at the center. 
The relationship between a parent and child cannot be broken by anything. Not even by an atomic bomb. It is a relationship that cannot be broken, separated, or discarded. 
Are all members of the Unification Church ready to welcome God? If I am not ready to be able to do so, I must become someone who can live and die by the command of the central figure. Families must stand in a position where they can live and die by the representative's command, and tribes must also stand in a position where they can live and die by the representative's command. Hearts and lives must be aligned with that standard and seek points of agreement. 
If the representative walks the path aligned with God's internal wishes, the whole will respond accordingly. 
In the future, if you are a member of the Unification Church, you must obey the Teacher's commands absolutely. If you cannot do that, you have no relationship with the Teacher. If you obey absolutely, you can receive the same benefits. 
To do so, you must have a communal sense of living together. 
All interests must be centered on the church. You must feel the same shock and pain. You may not qualify, but you receive the benefit of meeting God through the representative. 
There is no reasonable path for the condition of indemnity. There is no path that I can like. I must walk the path that the will can like. 
I have become this shape and form. Do not say that. Such recognition becomes anger. The question is whether this was a path that could be recognized and guaranteed historically. A life that has walked a smooth path without hardship and trials has a more profound and broader taste than a life that has gone through complex trials. 
The Teacher does not seek to establish a foundation. 
When have I ever had a moment where I could joyfully and confidently stand before God as a true parent? Have I ever had a time when I was flustered for God's work? God has walked many flustered steps. 
One must live like a mad person, muttering alone. 
The heart that a couple has when they give birth to an only son and die is God's heart beyond that. 
One must understand God's internal wishes, who loves the children of enemies more than his own. 
One must not feel a sense of face and prestige, nor should there be room to feel hunger or fullness. 
We must know God's internal wishes. 
One must be more concerned about the movement of the will than about one's own child being sick. If that is not the case, then at least obey absolutely. 
If you do not know what the Teacher is doing, you must live in such a way that you cannot sleep at night and must run to ask, even in the middle of the night. Thus, it is said that you are saved through the Teacher. The Teacher always lives like that concerning God. Not even a moment can be relaxed. Even when holding a baby or resting, that heart cannot be left behind. That is why everyone wants to live in Korea. To know the Teacher's news quickly. It is an honor to live by selling everything one has and just touching the land of the Republic of Korea. 
After striking my body, I must walk the path of indemnity that can comfort God. 
Let us establish a tradition. 
<Summary of the Words> Establish the tradition of the family. If one of the couple stands before God first, follow that person as the center. 
Which family is a model family? If a family cannot fulfill its mission, the entire family is at stake. And the ancestors in the spirit world will not be able to cooperate. 
A family must establish the tradition of Jesus and the Holy Spirit as reality for the nation, state, and world to establish their traditions. 
One must not be sad if one of the couple who stood in the will dies first. 
In that family, since the husband is the subject, he must take responsibility for the family. 
When evangelizing in the local area, one must put in three times the effort that was put into the family members. 
The Teacher could not sit with his legs stretched out. Also, the Teacher has never shown flesh in the world of Satan. Even in prison, he hid a washcloth and washed his body before morning prayer. 
Let us establish three traditions. 
1. The tradition in the family 2. The tradition in the church 3. The tradition in society 
Especially in the family, let us not frown. 
October 3, 1968 (Sunday), at the former headquarters church. 
* This message was given during a family gathering after the early morning worship service, organized from notes taken by former Association President Yoo Hyo-won. The title was added by the editor. 
7)
God's Inner World 
You think of God as good, holy, high, wide, great, and boundless. However, that is a good interpretation of God. 
The God who is responsible for the fallen world and is restoring it is not a God who resides only in high, precious, holy, and clean places. He has a miserable, painful, and horrific background that humans cannot even imagine or describe. 
However, no matter how difficult and painful it is, God has never appealed to anyone about that laborious situation throughout the historical process up to today. God has infinitely endured that difficult and sorrowful work. No one on this earth knows this fact today. 
In this way, God stands in a position opposite to what humans think, as a wide and great God. And in terms of endurance, no one has endured more than God, and no one has suffered as much as God has throughout history. 
Even with the inner suffering that humans cannot even guess, God does not show it before humans. 
We must understand that God is one who bears that difficult burden and groans without showing it, overcoming it, and not giving up on what He has planned, crossing over that hill and bringing forth a new providence of restoration. When we see this fact, we must recognize that there is a sorrowful underside to God that humans cannot possibly measure. 
The pain and sorrow of God reflected in the inner principles known by the Unification Church today is merely a very small part. 
We cannot even speak of suffering, labor, or difficulties while carrying such a God. 
If you ask me to talk about my suffering, I can share the stories of my hardships until now. However, as the chairman mentioned earlier, even those who have gone to the spirit world do not know, and there is a difficulty in speaking about the inner world that no one has discovered until now. However, such suffering is temporary. 
That suffering ends once it is done. When a problem is resolved, that matter is also finished. Therefore, that suffering is one that can see results in one's lifetime. However, God has been laboring for 6,000 years until now, but He has not been able to resolve it. 
No matter how much the Unification Church offers indemnity and restoration, the fundamental state of the heart that was shocked internally cannot be restored. That must be done by God Himself. 
Even if we, as children, try to comfort Him, we cannot provide solace. It must be done by God Himself. 
In other words, parents should be comforted by the words of their children, but that does not fundamentally comfort the parent's true heart. It is merely a condition for receiving comfort. Similarly, we must understand that God has been in such a position until now. Therefore, when we think of this, we cannot speak of suffering or difficulties. 
Before we suffer, God suffers greater suffering, and before we experience sorrow, God experiences greater sorrow, and we must understand how difficult the position of God is, who has the responsibility to save this sorrowful world today. 
We must recognize that God is in a more difficult position than the good meaning of God we think of. If we stand in a position to understand that deep inner world, then nothing is a problem. 
No matter how difficult one may claim to be, one cannot present that difficulty to God under any condition. If one thinks that God is in a position to present such conditions before us, we ourselves cannot endure it. 
When we think of the tremendous God who prepares our way before us and is concerned for us, we are carrying a double debt. Acknowledging that we must fulfill a double responsibility to settle this debt, I ask that you make this a motivation to overcome any difficulties on the path ahead. 
8)
The Responsibility of Blessed Families 
<Summary of the Words> Blessed families must feel the mission of influencing the whole. A family consists of a couple and children. It must not become a habitual family. The family is the point where the expectations of the son-in-law can be fulfilled. Here, the unity of the couple is required. They must align with the original standard that God desires. 
Heaven is established from the family. 
Blessed families are not made by themselves. They have a historical significance from God and centered on the Teacher. It is not achieved by themselves but is done externally. There was God's desire in this. 
The blessed family originated from the Teacher. Jesus also came for this purpose. 
God wishes for families that exceed the standards of families known to Him. 
The center of history is people. There are men and women among people. The relationship of the family that betrayed, that is, to restore one man and one woman. This is the original standard. 
God's original purpose in sending Jesus was here. Neither a man alone nor a woman alone can achieve completion. A family is essential. 
October 20, 1968 (Sunday), at 5:30 AM, at the former headquarters church. 
* This message was given during Sunday worship and is organized from notes taken by the chairman of the Association's History Compilation Committee, Yoo Kwang-ryeol. The title was added by the editor. 
As long as the family does not align with the original law, the hopes of the tribe cannot be fulfilled. 
How difficult is the blessing? The process is simple, but the content of the historical background is incredibly difficult. One cannot bypass this historical process. 
When he smiles, the entire universe can smile; this is the standard of blessing. 
We must correct our shortcomings and fulfill the loyalty of the couple that God desires. 
There is a lack of understanding regarding families. Men and women were born to represent heaven and earth. 
Everything is sworn around the blessing. Those who violate this oath cannot be accepted as existing on this earth. 
Heaven is established around the family. Family members must not forget the pride they must uphold. 
The position of Adam and Eve is one that can influence the universe, not one that is influenced. 
It must not be a habitual and secular family. One must not think, "It is like this now, but it will be fine in the future." It must already be perfect. The present is the issue. The past and present must be perfect for the future to be perfect. 
Not having such a day in the Garden of Eden is the evidence of the fall. A place where the past, present, and future can align is the ideal place. 
One must be able to dedicate the present. What God desires is whether it can become an eternal foundation on this earth. This is the historical synthesis point. 
One must realize the standard of the family. The man is the subject. The subject must stand in a subjective position, not in a relative position. He must stand at the center. This center must not be misaligned. One must maintain the center that can protect the position. This is the position instead of God. 
Motivation and cause start from the subject. Joy and happiness arise from the subject. If the family is in discord and unhappiness, the man must take responsibility. The responsibility for the fall must first be taken by God, second by Jesus, and third by the Holy Spirit. 
If one cannot establish that standard from the present position, one cannot stand forever. Even if it is achieved in the future, the days of that process will accuse. 
Heaven is established from the family. The rise and fall of our Unification Church can be influenced by the family. Even if a woman makes a mistake, the man takes responsibility. 
One must establish a mental standard and a living standard that does not deviate. Even when living apart, one must not be internally divided. 
Such Sunday worship time is solemn and precious. The Sabbath is a day to give glory before God. 
The Era of Salvation Centered on the Family 
One must overcome the resentment of the fall. One must receive the blessing and must not remain in that resentment. Ordinary families and our family are fundamentally different. 
Living for oneself is not for the family but must be for heaven and earth. The family must always win from a realistic standpoint and must never be subject to Satan's accusations. How many families can be like that? One must strive every day. 
To become a global nation, one must inherit the tradition. To become a nation that can lead the world, there must be such a traditional thought. 
Is there a tradition that can influence history and the world? It must not be absent. 
Just achieving individual perfection does not lead to global salvation. Jesus also came and died on the cross, but individual salvation could not be achieved, so He became the Triune God centered on God. Love must have a relative standard to be realized. 
If our Unification Church has something to leave as a tradition in world history, it is the standard of families that can align with heaven and earth. 
What tradition does the Unification Church aim for? That standard is the family. The source of victory and motivation can be the family. Thus, the love of the established families until now will also be judged. This is the judgment of love and the great judgment. 
When two couples become the East and West, they dominate all directions. The larger the radius, the greater the influence. Women must boast of men, and men must boast of women. 
If about 800 blessed families do well, our Unification Church will automatically expand. We must become families that everyone envies. Those who say, "I don't care about the will or anything," will perish. Those who think, "I came to the Unification Church, so I was blessed; did I want to be blessed?" will perish. 
If the family succeeds, all the historical turning points of failure will be as if they have not failed. Adam, Noah, Abraham, and Moses will all be revived. 
Children among men will say, "Our father is the best," and among women...
My mother is the best. We must establish a tradition that acknowledges this until the day we die.  
After the dawn worship, let us partake in communion with even the smallest things. We must leave a practical origin for this tradition.  
The family is the fruition of the historical desires of oneself, the teacher, and God. This is a blessing.  
When thinking of the other person, consider in the following order:  
① A thorough thought centered on the purpose, a pioneering path  
② Health  
③ Beauty  
④ Knowledge  
Until now, evangelism has been done alone, but from now on, couples must create children of faith together.  
The new historical era is an age of salvation centered on the family. A true era of evangelism for two is coming. The wife must think about how to make her husband a great person.  
One must become a noble ancestor in purpose.  
The family does not stop at the family level; it requires a lineage. Responsibilities as ancestors must be fulfilled. Those who receive blessings and are not in public office have gone astray.  
The wife must elevate her husband. In other words, she must support him well. Become the one who fulfills the Word (in substantial, emotional, and practical ways). The family is where God’s love, centered on the Word, blossoms.  
We must embrace history, the universe, and shed tears, sweat, and blood.  
Unity begins with the couple becoming one. If there is a male Messiah, there must also be a female Messiah, so the Lord comes as a familial Messiah. Since the fall was caused by Adam and Eve, restoration must also be done by both. This is becoming a tribal Messiah.  
The personal path of the teacher and the family’s path will become the tradition of future history.  
Couples who stake their lives for their families must become indispensable couples in the Unification Church. The descendants of Lee Wan-yong cannot claim their ancestors anywhere.  
The family that God desires, the family that the church desires, the family that you desire—children born in such families will be well born.  
Parents may suffer greatly, but their children will be born according to the fortune of heaven and the fortune of the teacher.  
Think of the three eras:  
① The Era of Eden  
② The Era of the Fall  
③ The Era of Hope  
If you prioritize the purpose and transcend all personal matters, God will cooperate.  
You must not act according to the body’s desires. Even if you are tired, you must not take a nap at will. You must not eat whatever you want just because you are hungry.  
If there are just three people praying for you in the background, even enemies cannot harm that person.  
Going down is preparation for going up.  
A loyal subject must be able to make the people weep. A good king must be appreciated by the people of all generations.  
You must become a family that is worthy of God’s desires, the desires of your ancestors, and your own desires.  
If you do not know the principle and have no accomplishments for the purpose, it will be truly difficult in the future.  
In the future, having noble ancestors in purpose will be a pride for the descendants.  
To establish the authority of the family, you must establish the authority of the individual, and to establish the authority of the individual, you must elevate the consciousness of authority regarding the purpose.  
Do not be indebted. Make double the effort. The teacher lives with the hope that even though the reality is like this now, one day among those blessed, the last remaining person will remain as a global human resource and receive glory.  
Do not sleep when others sleep, do not play when others play, do not eat when others eat; you must work.  
There is no time to rest while running toward the final finish line.  
The precious youth period in life  
<Summary of the Word> The youth period is the most precious time in life. It is the time when one can make a resolution to set a purpose. Therefore, the youth period is a turning point in life. Thus, one must plan their life around the age of 18.  
This era is like a crossroads in life. It is important to clearly understand how to proceed at this crossroads. The most important thing is whether one can smoothly transition through childhood, adulthood, and old age. Those who can smoothly transition through childhood, adulthood, and old age are pioneers.  
In life, there are joys and happiness that only one can feel. You must know that you are walking the path of restoration. Therefore, you must pursue the path of restoration and explore the story of restoration. If you walk the path of restoration well, you can find a new path that connects the universe and yourself. Thus, you can turn the historical sorrow into new glory.  
Fallen humans must make their utmost effort to meet the crossroads of life. That crossroads is the path to settle each person’s sorrow and, furthermore, to settle the historical sorrow.  
The path we started must be connected directly to the destination.  
And the current speed must be faster than the speed at the start.  
On October 27, 1968 (Sunday) at 6 AM, at the former headquarters church.  
* This word was spoken at the 4th National Spiritual Students’ Assembly and has been compiled from notes taken by former association president Yoo Hwa-ryeol and the association's history compilation committee chairman Yoo Kwang-ryeol. The title was added by the editor.  
To walk this path well, one must think of life as a short moment. Then, a sense of urgency will arise. That mindset must not change. Those who arrive at the destination and achieve victory, as well as those who have started, have not existed until now. However, you must not be like that.  
Korea must establish the tradition of everything and become the center of that tradition.  
The teacher established a path of indemnity through the first seven-year course. Therefore, we have now reached a time when we can surpass a period on the earth.  
What matters is what country, tribe, or parents you are a child of. We have not had a world of hope, a nation, parents, or siblings until now. But now we have a world of hope, a nation, a tribe, a family, parents, and siblings.  
Completion (成) means the perfection beyond creation. In other words, it signifies the completion of the entire universe. The time to set the standard of completion is the age when the human ancestors fell, which is 17 or 18 years old. Therefore, God wishes for everything to be achieved centered around the 20s of sanctification. Those who can occupy the position of future completion are the youth.  
The teacher set the standard of desire and life goals during the youth period. The teacher has now passed through youth and adulthood and is entering old age. However, one sad thing is that the teacher could not call out to the Father during the youth period. It is sad that he could not call out to the Father during the time like Adam and Eve in the Garden of Eden.  
For that reason, you are happier than anyone else.  
As one who has inherited God’s orthodoxy, you must go straight.  
The first seven-year course was a path for adults and youth. The second seven-year course is a path like that of Adam and Eve marching in the Garden of Eden. Therefore, you must move forward boldly.  
You must feel pity for students and teachers who do not understand the purpose. And you must think about how much effort God has put in to establish just one of you.  
What is not right must be subdued. To subdue force with something that is not force, one must make thousands of times the effort. You must establish the loyalty and integrity that can conquer any environment. And you must start with a pure heart and achieve your goals with unwavering steps.  
The principle is a traffic officer, and the goal of the principle is the life of the teacher. If you go toward the goal with all your heart, the traffic lights will appear. Each of you must make a historical start in your given environment. And you must sow and cultivate the seeds of truth.  
People in advanced Western countries find it difficult to feel restoration. However, we Koreans can feel restoration due to history and circumstances.  
Korea has started with everything prepared at once, so it can become the homeland of faith and the motherland. If you do not go straight from here, you cannot call yourself the youth of the homeland or the elder of the motherland.  
If I am lonely, I must make the surrounding students on my side. Then, I must be able to declare that I have conquered that school and I have won.  
Every time you look at your face in the mirror, you must ask yourself, “Are you walking the path you started before the purpose?”  
You must become those who do not tarnish the name of sanctification. When you can no longer do or endure anything by your own strength, only then can you say, “God, please help me.”  
You must become a self-reliant person.  
Become a true Adam and Eve with a sense of righteous indignation in the Unification Church. If you do so, it will become a church that is not ashamed to receive the blessings of the world.  
Even if all of you make a resolution together, the standards are different for each person. You must have the determination to listen to the questions of your nature and respond to the call of your nature to make a historical start. Thus, you must go steadily for 30 years without changing during that period. Those who strive like that will win. To do so, you must be single-minded, devoted, and unified in heart.  
The teacher holds on to one thing and does it with all his might.  
When the teacher was 16 years old, there were 13 family members, but only eight remained, and five family members died within a year. Such indemnity has been made throughout the historical process.  
Once you make a resolution, you must go until the day you die without changing. Those who do not have the determination to die cannot win. One cannot have the glory of victory if they fear death.  
If you do not take revenge on your enemies and instead pray for their blessings, something will remain there. Jesus’ resolution was made in a place of deep sorrow. That is the death of Jesus on the cross. Because Jesus prayed for blessings for his enemies even in that place, he was able to enjoy happiness with God. This is the way that is right yet successful. This is also the reason Christianity became a religion of martyrdom.  
Even in evil places, there must be something that can be endured. Even in a place of ruin, something must come out. Even from Satan, something must come out. If something comes out from here, you must have the determination to surely use it.  
Relative positions can fluctuate, but the central position cannot change or fluctuate. For example, the trunk of a tree is like that.  
Like fertilizer, everything has a good meaning in an indirect sense.  
The teacher wants to make everyone a sacrifice and offer them before God.  
After liberation, the teacher could not relax for even a minute. This was because he had to block the darkness of Satan from coming in. However, today, it has become possible for the purpose to be fulfilled even without the teacher praying.  
You must not be dragged by the environment but must lead the environment. Since you have started, go vigorously until the end.  
Ability only reflects one side, but sincerity is central, so it can reflect all sides.  
To place oneself in the highest position, one must be rooted in the lowest position. How wonderful and happy will it be to see you all breaking through the crossroads of life and running straight down the path?  
Establish the tradition of the family  
<Summary of the Word> When couples attend worship, they must come out warmly so that their children will want to follow them with envy. The fruits of the prayers of the saints must be borne in the family. The cultural level of a nation can be seen through family life.  
To become exemplary couples, at least one of the two must stand right. And when seeing a representative exemplary family, we must reflect on what score our family would receive.  
Blessed families are the targets of hope for everyone. However, if they do not fulfill their assigned responsibilities, they will become families of despair.  
Wives must take responsibility for solving economic issues within the family.  
Current blessed families are important because they are the ancestors of tradition. A messianic family must be established before the tribe for the tradition to be established.  
One must not wish for their sons and daughters to do well while failing to observe dawn worship, sincerity, and worship time. Therefore, centered on the teacher, one must fulfill the expectations of the son-in-law. And to establish descendants here, parents must do well.  
If one does not think, they cannot form relationships, and if relationships are not formed, they cannot establish connections.  
Parents must not give the impression that they are fighting in front of their children.  
On November 3, 1968 (Sunday), at the former headquarters church.  
* This word was spoken during a gathering of blessed families and has been compiled from what was published in the first issue of the <Newsletter> (dated November 15, 1968) and notes taken by the chairman of the association's history compilation committee, Yoo Kwang-ryeol.  
Couples must not engage in trivial fights saying, “You do not love me. You do not understand me.” Even if you fight, it must be for the purpose.  
The first seven-year course was a period for establishing individual traditions, and the second seven-year course is a period for establishing family traditions. If family traditions are not established, national traditions cannot be established, and if national traditions are not established, a nation cannot be formed.  
Blessed families must create family laws. And they must establish educational standards for their children and norms for the family. If parents have made mistakes and are questioned by their children, they will have nothing to say.  
Before loving oneself, one must love their country, the world, and God. The wife must be able to respect her husband by saying, “Our husband loves the country, the world, and God more.”  
In the family, the man must take responsibility for the trivial matters that arise. In other words, the man must maintain the central authority of the family.  
Blessed families, before you die and before you have children, you must establish family traditions. This means you should not wait until after having children to put in effort; you must put in effort even before giving birth. Children must be able to say that our parents are better than any other parents in some aspects. The more lacking they are in external aspects, the more unique authority they must have in some aspects.  
Children must be able to say that there are no parents in the world other than our parents.  
People from around the world will come to Korea to visit exemplary families. At that time, there must be something to show and something to say. Moreover, established families must change significantly from before.  
Children know whether their parents are good or bad. If you consistently push forward with an attitude of moving for the purpose, there will come a day when the environment will recognize you.  
Even if couples die, they must leave behind a legacy. What is the purpose of that family? Even if it exists for their children, it must first exist for God and the nation. Ultimately, that is the way to benefit their children. Only then can the children align with the fortune of God, the fortune of the world, and the fortune of the nation. Therefore, even if the precious children born from blessings suffer, do not align them with their own pace but align them with the fortunes of God, the world, and the nation.  
The fastest way to establish family traditions is to do so while the teacher is alive. Originally, one should bathe and cleanse every morning and walk ten miles to worship the teacher. If this tradition is not established, one’s descendants will perish.  
Sunday is a day to save and plan the week, providing content that can make our family happy. Also, Sunday is a day to gather and share prepared food and for each family to boast about their husband or wife.  
When going out to evangelize, one must put in three times more effort than the sincerity shown to the teacher. The more difficult it is, the better one must do. Established families must put in even more effort for their newly born children.  
Everyone looks up to the senior families as if they were heaven. Therefore, there must be something different from them, which is that the heart flowing in their marrow must be different. The couples of blessed families must become objects of admiration for others. How happy must a wife with such a husband be, or a husband with such a wife? They must be able to admire that.  
We must restore the family. There is no greater evangelism than this. Couples must rise early in the morning, hold their children’s hands, and pray with tears. Through this, when the father or mother is not around, the children must be able to wait for and miss their parents and sing.  
If one side of the couple leans, they must supplement it with heart and sincerity.  
From December 20, mobilize nationwide. The teacher did everything alone, but you have warm subjects to empathize with.
We must evangelize. If we go to the other world without evangelizing, we will hold onto each other as couples and weep bitterly. Thinking about that makes it impossible to sleep well at night. Blessed families should set an example by attending Sunday or public gatherings. Blessed families must evangelize on Sundays. They should arrive at the church before 10 AM on Sunday to prepare. No matter where you are or what you do, you must remember the worship time. And material offerings must go through the teacher's name. Do not live with an unpleasant face, whether day or night; get up with a smile, work with a smile, and go to bed with a smile. Do not take naps at your convenience. At the headquarters, one must never raise their voice. This place is where the true parents' connection was established, and something unprecedented in history has occurred in this house (headquarters church). The day we can worship here is not far off. **The Mainstream of Restoration**

**Prayer (I)** Today is the third Sabbath of this month. As we set the slogan of a full-scale advance before the Father, we must once again reflect on ourselves as individuals who must fight until we can embrace Your bosom while tracing the path of restoration entrusted with Heaven's solemn task. Father, this time is a holy day on which You can bestow blessings, and all people who seek Your high and precious mercy and love are gathered before Your presence. Among them, there are also children who are prostrating themselves with a heart of longing to fulfill the responsibilities entrusted by Heaven while pleading for a historical mission before You through Your heart.

It has been Your wish that countless individuals, families, and nations align with Your will, and we must think again about how sorrowful Your heart must be as You look upon the reality where individuals, families, tribes, and nations are not united. You have desired that countless multitudes bow down before You, but since there are no such multitudes, we know that You hope for even a small number to embody that appearance.

We hope that many individuals and families will be connected to such a place, but since that is not possible, we earnestly wish and hope that we may understand at this time that You are searching for true individuals and true families in this world.

Father, please remember Your children gathered here. We are insufficient beings, having nothing like naked ones. This was true in the past, and it is true in the present.

Before the one thought of Your hope, we are those who do not know how to manage our shameful appearances. Father, please cover our faults, and grant us hearts of compassion and mercy so that our insufficiencies may be fulfilled and our weaknesses made strong.

Father, there are many gatherings in this world, but among them, there are insufficient children gathered in humble circumstances. We do not come to possess You with the standard that You seek. You have ruled this earth and countless people with infinite authority and power, but we are hoping for the grace of Your mercy more than Your power. As we recall Your words and call You Father, please cause a revolution in our hearts so that our earnest desire to be embraced in the bosom of Your heart can explode, and bring about a change of heart so that we may be taken as God's own. We truly wish for that, so Father, please come to us.

Your circumstances must become our circumstances, and Your wishes must become our wishes so that Your heart and our hearts can be in harmony. Thus, when You are in sorrow, we must also be sorrowful, and when You are joyful, we must also rejoice.

We have gathered here longing to be able to unify with You as Your substantial counterpart, so please remove all that does not correspond to that and raise a nature of heart that can be completely in harmony and absorbed into it, so that we can be aware of being Your sons and daughters. We earnestly wish and hope for this time to work so that we can appear with the heavenly authority that is not shameful as Your children who have been established before Your will.

Our hearts must be unified as one, our work must be unified as one, and all our movements must be unified before the Father. Thus, may all of our entirety be able to be called children of God from the beginning to the end connected to You.

Father, how much have You labored to raise us until now? We have understood that You are the Father who does not mind comforting us a thousand times or ten thousand times with Your heart. We have come forth from the circumstances where You, forgetting Your dignity and face, held onto us and pleaded.

You have urged us not to perish, not to weaken, and to remain until the end, and as we think about whether we have become the substance of the fruits that can be suitable for Your commands and rejoice in Your commands, we cannot help but repent that this is also an unspeakable condition of lamentation before us that was the story of Your coming.

You came to give us the conditions of joy and happiness, but due to our irresponsibility, we have made You the Father of sorrow, the Father of grievance, and the Father who must bear accusations from Satan. We earnestly wish and hope that at this time, we may deeply repent of this fact.

Through thousands of years of history, how long have You awaited for Your wishes to be fulfilled on this earth? How long have You awaited for the appearance of true sons and daughters on this earth, and how long have You awaited for new families to appear? How long have You awaited for new tribes and new nations? At that place, may we become Your sons and daughters who can establish Your authority, dignity, and reputation, and may each of us feel that we must be those who can stand as such.

On this day, as the children of unification who are struggling under the burden of Heaven's time and mission, looking towards this place from all over South Korea, we earnestly hope that You will have compassion upon them. From the beginning to the end, we hope that You alone will preside and guide, and we earnestly ask that all our wishes be in harmony with Your heart and that we may all become one. Please grant us the remaining grace. I present all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen.

**Prayer (II)** Merciful Father, please make this place a holy sanctuary where our hearts can become one with Yours. May it be a sacred place where we can connect with Your heart, be immersed in Your circumstances, and fulfill Your wishes, where You alone can preside.

We know that those who are embraced in the bosom of the Father and Mother are truly happy. No matter how fierce the surrounding environment may be, and no matter if we live day by day on the brink of death, we know that a child sleeping in the arms of their parents feels the peace of heart.

We, who live in an evil world, a chaotic world, and a world where the waves of death surge, could not approach the Father, but even if it is just for that one hour when we can be embraced in Your bosom, we have come forth with longing, admiration, and desire, so we earnestly wish and hope that You will command us at this time.

Please grant us the nature of love that can resonate with Your heart, and with a heart of compassion, sanctify us so that all emotions flowing from our bones, hearts, and cells can become that which can resonate with You. May we feel the oneness between the wondrous You and us.

Thus, may this time be one where we can boast of Your greatness and rediscover Your preciousness, Father, and we earnestly wish and hope for this.

Father, please become the centerpiece and foundation of this gathering. May no one be able to pass through Your connection, and may no one be able to long for Your story. Only those who love You and have a relationship with You may be here, so please allow us to establish the subjectivity of life forever based on Your words, and may we be able to pioneer a new life.
I earnestly hope and desire that I may become a source of hope.  
134   The Main Current of Restoration

<Words> Today,  
I would like to speak briefly on the title of "The Main Current of Restoration."  
The word restoration means to return. To return means to have left the original place and to go back to that original place.  
What Religion Desires  
If humanity’s ancestors had started as good children centered on God, then we would not need the term restoration, nor would we need the term salvation. However, the need for such terms arose because humanity’s ancestors fell. Thus, humanity has been destined to walk the path of restoration.  
Today, countless people living on this earth are in a fate where they must be saved and regain their original posture. In the future, there must arise a decisive standard that determines the entire story of restoration and completes the purpose of salvation, whether it be an individual, a family, a tribe, a nation, or a country. As long as there is a relationship with God, heaven cannot appear on this earth before that happens.  
For this reason, fallen humans are pursuing a world of ideals, though they may not know what that is. They believe that an ideal world will appear before them on the path they are taking, but that is a great misunderstanding. From the moment they started, they did not possess the source to create an ideal world; rather, they began with the misfortunes of despair and hopelessness, and thus they are in an inevitable fate that must yield such results at the end.  
Today, many nations are aiming for one world, but when asked if that one world they desire will truly appear in this historical age, the answer is no. Why? Because humans started off incorrectly. It is an inevitable fact that a world equipped with the standard of truth cannot come before humans who carry a flawed history.  
Therefore, new ideals, new worldviews, new perspectives on life, and new loves with new lives cannot appear while being directly connected to the historical process that humanity desires. For this to manifest, the historical process must be settled at one stage. If it cannot be settled, it must return to the beginning and go through the process of searching again. This is the fate of humanity born as descendants of fallen humanity. Religion has come forth with this dual perspective.  
Thus, before the ideal world comes, there must be judgment. Those who can escape this judgment are not those who carry the historical circumstances and connections as they are, but those who abandon them. It is those who break away from such things and turn back to avoid the path who can escape judgment. Without this, a new idealistic beginning cannot be seen, which is why religion has taught us to forsake the world.  
Cut off all connections with the world. Do not draw close to the world. Do not reconcile with the world. Cut off from the world. From a negative standpoint, cultivate a new awareness.  
In light of this, we must feel that humanity is in a tragic fate where it cannot simply welcome the ideal world in the flowing historical process. We individuals standing in this historical authority must not simply follow this fate. We must either settle it or go against it. We must understand that both individuals and nations must pioneer this path of fate.  
Then, can this path be pioneered immediately on a national level? Absolutely not. A nation is formed beyond the standards of tribes. Can this path be pioneered immediately on a global level? Absolutely not. The world is formed through the processes of nations.  
So, where is the fundamental origin that can walk this path? There must be nations before there can be a world, and there must be tribes before there can be nations, and there must be families before there can be tribes, and there must be individuals before there can be families. Today, religious people who envision the ideal heavenly kingdom are crying out for salvation, but all of that is tied to the purpose of individual salvation. They pursue individual paradises, individual bliss, not family kingdoms, tribal kingdoms, national kingdoms, or world kingdoms. With that, they cannot enter heaven or bliss. A decisive and perfect standard must be established to save individuals, and a day must be set where an unprecedented foundation can be established in the historical age. Only then can one start anew as a new life and go to heaven or bliss.  
A Representative Model Must Arise  
When I look at myself placed in the currents of history that we must go through today, our mindset is eagerly anticipating a most magnificent ideal. This world is entering into an ideal world that forms a family realm. The emotions of the world can resonate with our emotions, and the circumstances of the world can connect with our breath.  
However, no matter how much external standards and forms are established, we cannot transition to the ideal world alongside this world. A historical model must emerge. Whether as an individual, a family, or a representative model that can stand on the principles of restoration centered on tribal, national forms, such a model must emerge. Without that model, we cannot transition to the ideal world. In other words, that model is the root itself.  
Throughout our history, many saints have come and gone. Why did they come and go? Did they leave a small wish in history because they wanted to live that way by their own will? Or was it the fate of history that made it so? If the fate of history made it so, then the fortunes of those ancestors become unnecessary. This must be judged. Furthermore, if those individuals left any contributions by their own will, that too is unnecessary for us. It must simply flow away.  
So, what kind of connection must be brought? One must bring a heavenly connection. Only those who have come with a heavenly connection, as beings related to the principles that require the story of God's restoration, can contribute and become a part of the process of developing into the world of historical hope today. Otherwise, all will be indemnified. No matter how great their contributions were in shaping today’s cultural world, those contributions will simply flow away. Then, where should the motivation and content be grounded? It must be grounded in a heavenly connection, not through one’s own efforts or the achievements born from the environment of the times. You must understand this.  
Whom does your heart seek? It seeks true people. Among the saints, it seeks true saints. Then, which is the highest reality? Which is the core of the main current? In other words, which stands on the first standard as a human? Today, even though academia and moral ethics represent such dimensions of standards, that decisive standard has not yet been established on this earth. Because of this, the purpose of hope that humanity desires has not yet been realized on this planet.

Because humanity stands in this position, what must God do? He must establish a standard in one person. If God had not announced such a decisive standard, then God does not exist.  
God loved the world so much that He gave His only Son, that whoever believes in Him shall not perish but have eternal life. (John 3:16) This statement is nothing more than an empty chant.  
In the end times of history, God must have a standard that cannot be announced; that is, the highest standard must emerge among humans. God is said to be a God of love, but when God created humans, in what position would He want to place them to love them? Among love, it is the love of spouses, the love of parents, and the love of children that He loves from the very core of these three loves.  
The Relationship of Love  
Humanity's ancestors fell, so they could not become sons and daughters centered on God. Since they could not become sons and daughters, they could not become true children. God is the same. When God loves humans, He must love them from the position of a son or daughter. This is an ironclad principle. God's Heart of Sorrow

Then, what kind of God is God? No. His heart would have been constricted, and all His senses would have been drawn into one place. was. Would such a God just watch while Adam and Eve ate from the tree of knowledge of good and evil? He had a sword and wanted to cut through history, to slice through this world, but He could only lament His own position where He could not do so.

<Word> Today is the 9th Children’s Day. What we must keep in mind every time our family celebrates Children’s Day is how precious this day is.

The Meaning of Children’s Day
After God created the heavens and the earth, He had to celebrate Children’s Day centered on Adam and Eve. If He had celebrated Children’s Day at that time, He could have established Parents’ Day from there, as well as a Day for All Creation, and God’s Day would have been designated.

So what kind of day is this Children’s Day? It is the day when children can triumph and enter the position of universal glory.

However, because humanity fell, since Adam, no one has been able to enter the position of glory that God could permit by winning in accordance with His will. Therefore, the history to restore humanity in such a position, the history to save them, that is, the history to bring them back to the original position, has been God’s providential history of restoration until now.

Then who is the Savior? The Savior is the one who comes to elevate fallen people to their original position. Children’s Day is not a day that is celebrated because it is particularly different from other days. Children’s Day is the first day that commemorates the fact that humans, who could not participate in the glory of God due to the fall, can finally participate in such a position after history.

If we follow those who have worked hard to bring us to this day, we can participate in such a glorious position. Therefore, today, if we members of the Unification Church follow the path that the Unification Church is taking, we will surely be able to stand in the position of the glory of children. Without celebrating this Children’s Day, we cannot receive salvation.

You will go to the spirit world. Jesus is also in the paradise of that world. However, Jesus must return to this earth. Why? Because He came with the mission of the Messiah from God but could not fulfill that responsibility, He must return. If someone goes on a business trip and finishes all their work, there is no need to go again. Because He left half of His mission unfinished, Jesus must return. Jesus could not participate in the position of glory as the Son of God because He did not fulfill all His responsibilities.

That is why Jesus has been praying until now. Prayer is what one does when what they hope for has not yet been realized, wishing for it to be fulfilled. It is asking God to provide strength to fulfill that. Therefore, to escape from such a place of demand, He must come back to this earth and complete His original mission. Without doing so, He cannot enter the position of victory.

Today, Christianity says that Jesus accomplished everything by dying on the cross, but that means He achieved spiritual salvation through His death on the cross, not complete salvation of spirit and body.

God’s ideal of creation is not to create a spiritual kingdom. He intended to establish a kingdom on this earth centered on Adam and Eve. Of course, He also wanted the children of Adam and Eve to live as citizens of the kingdom. However, throughout history, no one has established such a standard. Therefore, such families could not appear.

The Core of Truth is Father and Mother (Parents)
However, the fall did not happen solely because of Adam or solely because of Eve. Adam and Eve fell together. Thus, Adam and Eve became the ones who sowed the seed of resentment before God. Therefore, to uproot what they sowed, it must be done by both of them.

That is why Jesus came to this earth and established the standard of bride and groom. It is to completely uproot the bitter roots of sin that Adam and Eve sowed. To do this, He must come in the position of a parent and recreate the position of Adam and Eve on this earth and uproot it. Then who is the bridegroom Jesus? He is the Savior, but He is not an older brother; He must be in the position of a father. In other words, He must be in the position of a father who can directly give birth to us.

It is said that if you believe in Jesus, you will be resurrected. Resurrection means that life is born again. There is no way for life to be born again through an older brother. Without a relationship between a father and a son, one cannot be reborn. That is why Jesus is the Father, and the Holy Spirit is the Mother. The Holy Spirit spoken of in today’s Christianity is the Mother Spirit. Since Adam and Eve became false parents due to the fall, they must be restored to become true parents. However, if Adam and Eve had not fallen, becoming true parents would have been simple. The standard of human history is also simple.

Then what is the content of truth? No matter how good the content of truth is, it cannot replace one’s own mother and father, and no matter how good the content of truth is, it cannot replace one’s husband or wife, nor can it replace one’s children. What is the highest truth among truths? It is parents, spouses, and children. There is nothing beyond that. So what is the center of truth? It is love. When viewed through this principle, what is the center of the highest truth?

People say that God is the embodiment of truth, the embodiment of goodness, the embodiment of love, and the embodiment of life, but what does that mean? They are all the same. For truth to be established, love and life must be present.

For a person to be able to speak of true truth, they must have a desire and aspiration for truth within their life. Here, desire is relative to one’s own standard of character.

Therefore, what is the most essential core? The embodiment of life, the embodiment of love, and the embodiment of truth is God, and who is God? He is our human Father and at the same time our Mother. The core is parents. When viewed this way, God is a simple being.

We Must Love Jesus More Than Our Own Lives
So what has Christianity been doing for 2,000 years? It has been preparing to receive the bridegroom. The bride and groom must come among the people of this earth, with the bride being the Mother and the groom being the Father.

Then why do we need the Father and Mother again today? Because we humans were born wrong due to the fall, we must be reborn. That is why there is the term "born again."

You were born, but you are in a position as if you were born without parents. Therefore, you must go back into your mother’s womb and be born again. This has been the history of salvation until now.

To achieve salvation, both the Father and Mother must come together, but until now, only the Father, Jesus, has come. Jesus is the Father-like Savior, not an older brother-like Savior. So what should people who believe in Jesus do today? They must enter into the position of the seed of a son or daughter that is hidden in the bones of a bachelor before marriage. What will they do by believing in Jesus? Christians should strive to be like Jesus. Thus, they should become one with Jesus. Jesus must be in me, and I must be in Jesus... What does this mean?

Jesus has not yet married. So where does Jesus go? He goes to seek the seed of a baby that is in the man who has not yet entered the position of the bridegroom. And what must He do? He must give birth to that baby through the body of the bride, that is, the body of the mother. Without doing this, one cannot be born again. This is what is spiritually working in Christianity through the work of Jesus and the Holy Spirit.

Therefore, those who have not received the Holy Spirit cannot be reborn, and without going through the mother’s womb, one cannot atone for sin.

Then why does the Holy Spirit perform the work of washing away sin? Because the Holy Spirit is the Mother Spirit. Since Eve, the mother of fallen humanity, sowed sin, the Mother Spirit must come to wash away that sin. Therefore, according to the principle of atonement, the Holy Spirit comes to this earth to perform the work of washing away sin. Then what will happen after washing away sin? Humanity must be brought into a position where the Father can freely possess them, that is, they must enter into the position of the seed of a son or daughter that is in the bones of Adam before marriage.

That is why humanity must love Jesus more than their own lives. They must become one with Jesus. Both men and women must love Jesus. Men must long for Jesus to the point of forgetting themselves, and women must long for Jesus to the point of forgetting themselves. This is not a worldly matter. Is longing for one’s mother a worldly matter? Even if one’s husband or wife dies in this world, they must be able to say that they will not let go of Jesus.

In our Unification Church, when we say it is Children’s Day, this is not a simple matter. Everyone, children are male and female, right? What happens when you reverse the word "children"? Living a life centered on God's purpose

So, where can we find the true life, the life that can be a model? To find that, we must give up our limited individual perspectives. We cannot hold onto any of our individual desires, purposes, consciousness of life, or emotional states. All of these belong to a limited realm. While they may work within that limited environment, they cannot relate to God's purpose, which must go beyond. Since we are ourselves limited within this environment, the habits and attitudes we have in this realm cannot align with the eternal purpose God aims for.

So, what about us today? In our current state, we cannot establish a model based on any of our claims. In other words, because we have not reached such a position, we cannot live with a subjectivity centered on ourselves.

The day we achieve complete restoration and can establish our subjectivity is the day God's creation purpose is fulfilled. What kind of place is that? It is a place where Satan cannot accuse on this earth, a place where God's glory can completely harmonize with all of our beings and ourselves. When we think of such a place as the goal God aims for, we must recognize that the current realistic stage of the world we live in is in stark contradiction to God's intended purpose. Considering myself, who remains in this realm, when I establish principles and origins of a model centered on myself, it is ultimately just my own claim. Since it starts from oneself, it bears its own results and has no relation to God.

Then, where should this standard originally be established? It should not be established centered on oneself but centered on God. When we establish this standard centered on God, the starting point also begins from God, so the process must proceed with God, and the endpoint must also be connected with God.

We must take God as our model.

God has brought forth the wheels of history through a long historical process, transcending time and space in an infinite world. In contrast, we live in a limited environment. Because of this, all our environmental conditions are very far from that infinite world. Therefore, every single one of them cannot help but conflict.

New Awareness  
<Prayer> Father, this morning is the Sabbath. Please allow us to encounter your glory with our children, to encounter your high and precious personality, and to make this morning a time when we can experience the victorious will of your desire.  
Father, when we think about the fact that your creation of the entire universe has been so violated by the ancestors of humanity, the more sad things pile up, the more we must feel that we are unworthy before you.
must be established on the foundation of a new ideology for a tribe to form. Therefore, before we can envision a nation, we must first build a new family.

As we reflect on our responsibilities, we must understand that our actions today will shape the future for generations to come. The legacy we leave behind will be determined by our commitment to embodying the values of the new ideology in our families, tribes, and ultimately, our nation.

In conclusion, let us commit ourselves to this noble cause, working tirelessly to establish new families, tribes, and nations that embody the principles of the new ideology. Together, we can create a brighter future for all.
In order for this to be born, there must also be an individual who has a new awareness. Without personal awareness, one cannot become a new individual, nor can a new family be formed. 

From this perspective, when we look at our Unification Church today, there must be individuals who have the new awareness that God desires, and through those individuals, a family must be formed. Furthermore, through that family, tribes must be formed, through those tribes, nations, and through those nations, a state and a world must be formed. We must newly realize that such a higher system is connected to our individual selves. 

The Work of the Aware
When comparing with some historical saints or when we encounter them, we cannot establish a new history unless we become a reality that can decisively determine the awareness and resolution we have. 

From this perspective, when we compare the position of our Unification Church today with the positions of past patriotic figures who, centered on their thoughts, ideologies, and lifestyles, resolved to love all people of the nation and the world, we cannot overcome historical figures of such stature, nor can we establish the era or create a new future. It goes without saying that if this happens, we will not be able to see the start of a newly aware world. Therefore, we must stand in a position beyond that. 

Many revered saints have come and gone throughout history. Figures like Jesus, Confucius, and Buddha have come and gone. They looked at the corruption of the times and the social environment and sought to push that society away and to clear it out from the opposing position. They sought to establish a new realm centered on their social views, national views, family views, and views of character. We must recognize that there was adventure involved in that. 

The more difficult the environment, the more the saints who appeared with a new awareness had to face adventure. Furthermore, there was the adventure of the nation, the adventure of the ethnic group, and the personal adventure that collided with them. Therefore, we must not be in a lonely position, dominated by the incoming environment, but must have a character centered on an aware heart that can overcome that incoming environment. No matter how terrible the environment may be, if that character does not change, one can remain an aware being capable of resolving that environment. 

We know that countless saints have fought against the environment with their lives. If Jesus walked that path from an aware position, did Jesus himself have the family, tribe, nation, and world of that aware position? He did not. While Jesus had an inner desire for a nation and world, he did not possess a substantial, realistic nation or world and died on the cross. Therefore, Jesus must return and establish the desired nation and world he envisioned in reality. In other words, Jesus has a mission to create a new world on this earth that can be boasted of within his realm of life, and he must return to fulfill that mission. 

So, what position do we, who are aware today, hold? We must inherit the world of hope that Jesus desired and take responsibility to realize it within our realm of life under realistic social foundations, facing that world, nation, ethnicity, family, and individuals with a belief more aware than Jesus. Without standing in such a position, it is a given that we cannot establish the desired kingdom of heaven on this earth. 

Therefore, when we say that our Unification Church has an ideology that can unify the entire universe or world, those who are aware within that ideology will have the authority to connect numerous saints and sages in a dignified position, as mentioned above.

All the efforts made in the past must be harvested in the present. All the efforts made in the present must be harvested in the future.
