Therefore, as the fruit of the three stages, it can be said that the realized self has been established centered on this substantial world, and it can be said that such content has been determined before the universe, without which one cannot stand in the past, present, and future.

To pass through the cosmic crossroads, what has been hoped for must be determined in reality. The past bears fruit in reality, and the future must also see the starting point in reality. Moreover, the present must start from here. At some point in the flowing historical era, these three points of the historical process must intersect around our personality. If you do not have such decisive authority, you cannot enter heaven.

So what should be done? The way of life must fundamentally change. Therefore, there will inevitably be conflicts. Wherever the Unification Church goes, there will inevitably be conflicts. However, one must not retreat from the environment of conflict. One must break through.

As a newly realized self, you must innovate society with conviction and establish a standard of transition into new fields while binding the world of evil. In some sense, by determining that newly realized position, new selves, new families, new tribes, new nations, and a new world can be realized, leading to a new history.

From this perspective, the history that the Unification Church has walked until now cannot be compared to the history that has walked for thousands of years without knowing the will. Although the history of the Unification Church is short, it must have the realization that it cannot be judged by any historical figure or the history of thousands of years. In this sense, you should not forget the value of history that the Unification Church holds and should not take a position that emphasizes the contents of the past history of Israel like those who only believe in Jesus.

People often forget their own value and have a desire to supplement their value from others. While it is inevitable to have an inner desire for global development, that is not the essence. One must clearly recognize their own value and add to it. Without this understanding, one cannot add to it and cannot become the master of history. If a person is drawn out by history and the environment but has the intellect to digest and correspond to it, that may be different...

Today, when viewed in light of the history of our Unification Church, that history, though short, possesses a value that has not existed in any historical process. We must think that we are historical descendants who can praise the value of the new historical era.

In South Korea, one should praise national treasures or anything that can serve as the cultural background of the nation, but more than that, one must praise the substance that can remain in the new historical process. When we look at the history of the past 100 years that we have walked, we must value what has been left behind from the past to the present more than anything else. One must become a person who can appreciate that. Those who forget and lose it are selling their currently realized selves.

Recently, it was reported in the news that hundreds of precious paintings from Korea were sold to a foreign land by a Japanese sect. Consider that the paintings are in a foreign land that is not their homeland. That is a loss for the nation.

The value of the Unification Church
In light of this, the historical value that the Unification Church has walked until now, bearing the mission of restoration and completing the internal mission of 6,000 years of history, corresponds to infinite value. Yet, many people forget this.

Today, within this country, there are national treasures or precious national treasures that can be recognized as such in any country in the world, but among the short history of the Unification Church, there are national treasure-level events that can be accepted by all people for thousands of years. However, many people forget that value. Such people cannot be seen as those who can establish a new historical era. Therefore, we must realize that the history of the Unification Church has a value that can shine brighter than past history, and we must recognize that our current position holds infinite value compared to any social or living sphere of this era.

Then, when comparing that realized position with current standards, is the realized position better in every aspect? It is not. Externally, it may be worse than the present. However, when viewed as a whole, which is more valuable? Externally, one cannot see that value. It may appear miserable, unfortunate, and pitiful, but one must realize that it holds more value than anything in the current world. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."

Even if you wander in the streets, or live in difficult circumstances worse than anyone else, the realized value you possess at present can shine for thousands of generations better than the value held by any person in the historical era. Therefore, if you do not stand in a position that God can recognize, you will become someone who sells the current value. Not knowing the value of one's national treasure and selling it, whether it be South Korea or Japan, is akin to selling off one's country's precious items. They will face historical condemnation in the future.

At this point, we must hold the value we possess as infinite and shine that value for thousands of generations before the universe. And we must go out with the confidence that we will adapt to any historical value better than any other. No matter how unattractive or miserable that position may be, its value is cosmic. Even if one dies in a foreign land, that body is not just a body that died as an individual. It is a body that has died in a position that can leave a historical value for the new era, and you must clearly understand that.

Therefore, all the facts solidified within our living sphere must be recognized as a realized environment that cannot be exchanged for anything that could bring luxurious happiness to this world. This is why tears flow here and why difficulties intersect here. Those difficulties and tears become an internal experience that is more than sufficient to conquer the era. Without that, a new world cannot be achieved. In other words, without that, this world cannot be transformed into a new world.

You must feel the current value
From that perspective, one must not despair just because external standards are disconnected. One must also not stand in a backward position. You must understand that you cannot skip that stage. You must become those who know that the realized value of the present is more precious than any realistic value in the world.

Even the back yard of our Unification Church is more precious than the luxurious places of any high-rise building, places that everyone can see as sacred. Therefore, you must feel that even a speck of dust or a breath of air here holds infinite value compared to anything in the world.

So, do you agree? Those who enter the headquarters church often say, "Oh, it's frustrating. Oh, it's frustrating." Some people come here and find all the good rooms uncomfortable and just go out to sleep. However, once you truly understand that value, even if you are told to go out and sleep, you will not go. What is gathered here is not everything. Those who cannot feel the sensation within this living sphere will be left behind.

Those who can infinitely feel the current value can create the world of the future and leave the authority of the future. However, those who do not know the current value cannot relate to the value of the future world, no matter how great it may be. You must clearly understand that fact. The future cannot exist without passing through the present, so those who cannot infinitely feel the value of the present cannot inherit the infinite value of the future.

You must understand that the current value of our Unification Church is based on the position centered on the will. You must start from that position toward the future from this moment onward. When the teacher's words end, those words already enter into the future.

Everything until now is being settled by the future history. In other words, it is not the present that settles the present, but the future history that settles it. Everything that has been in the past and present is settled by the future history. The future speaks of what is to be done from now on. When two people speak, that already establishes a relationship of give and take, creating the future.

Where does good and evil arise, and where are good and evil determined? They are determined in the processes of the present and the future. They are not determined in the processes of the past and the present, but in the processes of the present and the future.

Those who are pushed out in the present cannot be settled in the future
Here, one must discover that the quantity of good in the present and future is greater than the quantity of good in the past and present; otherwise, one cannot remain as a being of the realized world. Therefore, one must recognize that what separates the present and the future is our current self.

We must seek a greater future world, so if we do not plant the greater future value in the reality process even in the environment that is behind us today, we cannot become the masters of the future world. If we continue to think, "That's enough for today, that's enough for tomorrow," and focus more on tomorrow's value than on the value of reality, we will fail.

Therefore, we must realize the connection between the past and present centered on the present and possess an explosive driving force that can start with a stronger, more hopeful, and more thorough determination than the present. Only then will the world of the future come before us. However, those who are despondent about the present will not be welcomed by the future. Those who are pushed out in the present must be settled now; they cannot be the standard for starting in the future. Only by pushing away the difficulties of the present and enduring the labor can the standard for the future be established. Thus, one must understand how important reality is.

When you wake up and open your eyes, they say today comes. The coming of today is different from the past's authority connected to yesterday and now. Because today comes, tomorrow immediately approaches us.

Today, my personal position seeks the position of tomorrow's family, and today's family position seeks the position of tomorrow's tribe. Likewise, today's tribal position seeks the position of tomorrow's nation, today's national position seeks the position of tomorrow's world. To pursue a greater field and to embrace and support it, there must be a more robust and powerful stimulating foundation. And there must be a united heart in pursuing that.

However, for one year, two years, or perhaps the first three years, one may take root and work hard but then stop. That is similar to dogs or pigs. When spring comes, dogs or pigs jump around happily. But then, when summer passes and winter comes, they say, "Oh no!"

We must rest, but we must not rest without timing. We must sleep, but we must not sleep without timing. We must rest and sleep to grow bigger and stronger. Then, even if the world that will judge you tries to take your past that started from the Unification Church, it cannot take it away.

The current position of the Unification Church cannot be drawn into any reality. No one can swallow the Unification Church. No one can conquer the members of the Unification Church. Furthermore, the path of hope that the world has longed for cannot be without the Unification Church. There can be no other way.

The history of the past was more brilliant than our current history. Therefore, we are educating in this way. When viewed from the perspective of national history, we can establish standards for teaching history, such as "This is why the history of South Korea failed," or "This is why the ancestors of America prospered." We can establish these as standards that can settle the era. You must stand in a position where you can do that.

Become the main actors of the restoration history
Until now, you have come into the Unification Church and lived with devotion for God. There were times when you struggled to fulfill the will, and there were moments when you thought, "Why do I have to do this alone when no one else does? I'll just follow along." This is akin to selling off the foundation you have built until now. It is the same as an individual selling off everything that could become a national treasure. The movements of your past do not remain with just one individual. They belong to the nation and the world, shining brightly in the history of the Unification Church. Yet, there are many individuals who selfishly sell them off. Do you know of such people? They are selling off treasures that can be boasted of to the nation and the world.

From the spiritual world, the teacher is speaking important words. In fact, this...
The same words should be delivered as a sermon, but I am speaking about it now. You all go out and come back, just nodding and dozing off, but the content of the words should never be something to doze off about. Dozing off is like selling the words in the spiritual realm, so if you feel sleepy in any organization, you should quickly leave. Why does that organization become a minus (-) for you? It would be better not to go at all. 

There are people who doze off thoughtlessly. They should not rot the speaker's insides. You may be tired, but the teacher is also tired. The teacher woke up at two in the morning. So, it's the same level of tiredness. 

Everyone, how precious is this time today? When you get exhausted, you are selling your own treasure. Yet, you might say that you have been starving for a purpose for several years. How many of you have experienced hunger? Raise your hands. There are many. Anyway, raise your hands. This is our situation today. The teacher has also eaten a lot of rice. We must have the same heart as the leading actors on stage. When tears flow in a scene, it means becoming a member of that family. When witnessing that, your heart should ache and you should weep. Those who feel moved are like the leading actors. 

Imagine that you have become the leading actor in the restoration history. How wonderful is it to receive food just by asking for it? Wow, a new righteous person has appeared at this historical moment. When you have that value, even the ladies will treat you well. However, food! To receive food? Oh, how embarrassing. As a man, to be receiving food, my grandfather said that no matter how poor one is, one should not become someone who receives food, and my father said the same. Yet here I am, going around receiving food in the Unification Church! People who are staring blankly at distant mountains will fail. 

Such people will not last long. They won't last three years, or even seven. They say they will go, but they are packing their bags behind the scenes. Of course, there is much hardship. But how wonderful is that hardship? How wonderful it is! God comes to those who are suffering. 

That is why the history of the Unification Church is more precious than the history of the world. You must understand that. 

Suffering for a purpose is a treasure. How many people are there who, in the process of founding the history of the Unification Church, have inherited all the time that has moved until now, cherishing it as their treasure and striving to leave it as the treasure of their family? 

I have worn work shoes or sneakers until the tops were intact but the soles were gone. I had no choice. I was in a position to go around receiving food, so could I buy new shoes? My toes were filled with dirt, but I wore them. Yet, how good that taste is! 

When will you ever do that for the purpose? The shoes I wore while walking are materials that can eloquently speak for a thousand years. If there is no present time to settle that moment, our ideology cannot resonate in front of the existence of this world. For the fragrance to resonate, the wind must blow. In a spring garden where warm winds do not blow, the fragrance cannot resonate. The spring breeze must scatter in all directions for the fragrance to resonate. Our ideology is the same. The teacher speaks because he knows that. 

When the teacher was in prison in Hungnam for about three years, he wore clothes from the ammonia fertilizer factory, which became unwearable, and took all the undergarments to make a bundle of rags to cover himself and sleep. Then people would gather around. If the world had seen it, they would have thought, "That guy will end up selling rags!" So, he kept all the clothes he wore for three years intact. And he came out with that bundle of rags. If that remains in the Unification Church today, it would be a global treasure. It may seem worthless, but if it exists, it will continue to speak silently for eternity. Do you understand what I mean? 

How precious is the reality that can unearth such treasures? When I become aware of the value of my historical mission, the path I walk will remain as a standard for future generations to follow in history. In a garden full of twists and turns and many stories, the tangled area of those stories will broadcast to the world forever. How precious is that moment that can leave behind a shining value? You must understand how precious it is to struggle in a place where you are trying to save heaven and earth at the crossroads of a wretched death. 

The suffering that can plant infinite value. You will also become ancestors in the future. Therefore, you must leave behind treasures that your descendants can proudly uphold for eternity, even in the current difficult living conditions. You must understand that this is your current position. 

The more comfortable the external environment is, the greater that value becomes. If the external environment must be lonely, sad, and filled with grievances and frustrations, and if the hardships you endure in that place become global hardships, then that one incident can completely conquer the world. In such a position, the motivation and the wealth and treasures that can completely subjugate the world are unearthed. Thinking that I am going through such a moment, even if a whip comes behind me or a spear tip comes to my chest, I could not lament. 

The current suffering becomes infinite value. Even if the teacher tries to betray and despair, the historical mountains of the past need me, so I cannot do that. The tangled relationships of the present are so immense that I cannot help but carry them all. As time approaches, thinking that the world flows in connection with me, I cannot afford to think differently to set history in the right direction, nor can I afford to get tired. 

My current mission and position cannot be exchanged for money or anything in the world. The fact that I can plant and leave behind infinite value that is the only one in the world here is tremendous and precious. You must understand that you cannot come into the Unification Church and just nod off without knowing this. 

People generally seek the values that appear in reality. The source of life is not in what appears. 

Everyone, what do you think the source of life is? Does it appear? Do you know where your source of life is? Is it in the heart? It is not the heart. The source of life is not well understood. The value related to treasure is not in the crowd gathering and saying, "Wow!" It is all hidden in the unknown. 

Greatness is not created when everyone comes and says, "Wow!" When people say "Wow!", it is already just a shell. That greatness begins from decades ago, when the time cannot be known. 

When looking at a tree, where is the value of the tree? One might say that it has value in being cut down for use or for building a house, or that even the dead tree itself has value for human use, but that is a misconception. The life value of the tree itself is in the roots that do not appear. No matter how lush and abundant the leaves are, they will all fall off. No matter how good the branches are, they will be cut off. However, the roots cannot be cut off. Right? You must understand that. 

Today, the Unification Church must have a new awareness in front of the path it must take. If you do not know how infinite the value of what has been started until now is, you will inevitably sell all your treasures and say, "Oh, that was a treasure that is unmatched in the world." That day will surely come. You may not know your own value, but you must live to recognize that value and to reclaim it as your own. When countless people are willing to pay an infinite price to acquire it, if you do not know that value, you could easily become someone who sells it for a penny. 

Are you in such a position, or are you not? Which side are you on? From what I see, most of you are likely to be in such a position. 

Even when the teacher says to do public work today, some say, "Oh, is there anything to gain from doing public work? My children are starving, and no matter how hard I work, there is not even a drop left." Some people say, "Hey, I will give you 10,000 won. Tell the teacher that I have something to do today." And they rush over there. There are many such slackers here. They are insubordinate, traitors who sell history and sell the nation. If the Unification Church teacher had done that, what would have happened? 

Thinking that the past, present, and future of the Unification Church can sprout with infinite value, I must plant the tree I have sown and say, "May it grow well for thousands of years!" I must plant the purest things. I must select and select to plant the true ones. I must plant true seeds that cannot fail to sprout in sacred places. I must plant them with blood, sweat, and all my sincerity. 

Let’s awaken anew. 

If we put our sincerity into it, it is certain that God will come to this place. And when we can offer all the ultimate historical values and what I have laid down in that path to God, we can become eternal sons and daughters of God. In that sense, you must be those who can recognize. Do you understand what I mean? 

The historical past has passed, and the current era is flowing without leaving anything behind. Many present moments have flowed into the past. In God's ideal world of creation, there are no museums. The enemy's group must be completely burned away. 

However, in the future, the Unification Church can remain centered on the connections of history. In the garden that God hopes for, in the center of the nation that God hopes for, precious treasures that can enter the museum are beginning to emerge in the current environment of our Unification Church today. 

Therefore, we must have a new awareness in reality. That is why it is an infinite personality, an infinite family, an infinite tribe, and an infinite ideology. Thus, feeling fulfilled here, living here, fighting here, and shedding tears here becomes an infinite worldview, and the hardships endured here remain as the contributions of the infinite world. When I think of this, where could there be anything more fulfilling? Since I know my value, it is only natural to seek that value, regardless of what the world may say or how it may criticize. 

Let’s say there is a diamond mine here. If there is a place that only you know about, what would you do? Would you apply for permission without others knowing? You might even have to sell your family for that. If you sell your wealth to save many families, that is not a sin. If you sell your child to save many sons and daughters of the country, that is also not a sin. However, you must not sell for your own greed. Therefore, if that mine is the way to save this country and this nation, and the way for people all over the world to live, then it is not a historical sin to have sold your wife and children to obtain permission. It may seem that selling your wife or children to save the nation or the world is wrong, but rather, there can be the source of treasures that the world can praise. 

Everyone, let’s think. What kind of path are we on right now? It has been said to be the final path. Therefore, we must be able to feel that fulfillment infinitely. We must once again have a new awareness. You have been doing things every day that will be judged from a historical perspective until now. 

In that sense, you must understand that a new awareness is needed. Do you understand? "Yes." 

<Prayer> Father, even if we hold our hands empty, we know that we possess infinitely. 

Father, we thank you first for the hard path you walked until the Unification Church was born in this world. The Unification Church did not come this far by gathering wealth. We have walked this path leaving behind our bare bodies, traces of tears, and marks of terrible wounds. However, knowing how much you have labored to leave this gathering and this organization, I cannot help but thank you once again. 

Father, we started with empty hands, but now we stand in a position where we envy nothing. We do not need money, we do not need power, and we do not need any culture of the world. More than that, what we crave while starving is God's love, parental love, spousal love, and children's love. We seek a family centered on the Heavenly Father in the homeland where the heavenly land can rejoice. Father, is there anything more valuable than such a family? Even if gold and treasures are as abundant as mountains, what connection can surpass that of a family centered on parental love, or the connection of siblings centered on parents? 

Knowing that you have come to find this, we earnestly hope and desire to be the ones who can leave behind infinite value here, to enjoy here, to pledge here, and to connect the motivations to establish history as the soldiers of unification. 

In the long historical process, we have shed sad tears. In every environment where men and women meet, sad stories have passed by, and on the crossroads of history, we know that they have evoked the sighs of heaven. Therefore, today we earnestly hope and desire that men and women can form a united family to fulfill your sorrow and become a solid bridge to defend against the enemy. 

From that standpoint, we must find ourselves, find our families, find our tribes, find our nations, and run toward a newly awakened world. 

When we realize that we are the ones who must go without rest today, may we know how to pave the way for tomorrow even in our sleeping places, and when we think that tomorrow's path remains in today's arduous labor, may we forget today's fatigue and think of tomorrow, overflowing with hope, and go forth centered on heaven and earth. 

If one’s strength is weak, may they be supported by the strength of heaven, and if one is lacking, may they become your children who know how to borrow the strength of the earth as they go forth. 

Father, today is the Sabbath. Many people who call upon your name and follow you have heard the command to keep the Sabbath holy, but many are moving while forgetting their own mission to serve you.
Father, please protect your young children gathered here today. Although today is a holy day, even if they are not able to keep it as a holy day and are in a place where they cannot attend at this time, please comfort their hearts and watch over their paths. May this place be a place of offering for this nation and a place of worship before You, and may we feel this even more deeply. With tearful hearts, let us once again connect our activities to the capital city of Seoul this morning.

Please do not let our walk be pitiful or shabby, but let us march as your children, strong and courageous heavenly warriors who can conquer the world, attacking and charging against the enemy in loyalty to Your command. We earnestly hope and desire this. When sorrow overflows and pierces our bones and flesh, please allow us to embrace You in our hearts, and in places where tears intersect, do not let us weep for ourselves, our families, our nation, or our ideologies, but let us be able to shed tears for families, tribes, nations, and humanity centered on You, and let us become new workers who can compile a new history of heaven. 

We earnestly hope and desire that this time, those who truly love You will worship and offer praise before You. 

From now on, for the remaining time, wherever we go, may You be with us, Father, and let us love You with unwavering hearts and work for the development of Your will. We earnestly hope and desire that we may not become those who lose the position You have established for us as liberators to restore the nation and liberate all people of the world.

Father, please let us know that all the facts of remaining history are looking upon us, and let us realize that countless nations and many sovereign states are calling upon us. 

Even if our feet are wounded, we know that we have a mission to lead those feet, so let us be Your sons and daughters who can struggle to go toward that place. We must go even in the dark of night, we must go even in our dreams, and we must go while we are awake, believing that You will be with us on the path we carry our mission. 

Since we share the same circumstances and positions as You, we know that the path we walk is a place where Your tears follow, where Your sighs can be felt, and where Your difficulties and loneliness can dwell. Also, because that path can be the closest place to You, we know it is a place where You can come and comfort us. Even if we must die a thousand or ten thousand times, please allow our hearts to long to die with Your comforting voice. 

We want to go to the place where we receive Your commands and are comforted by You. Even if it is a place of whipping, even if it is at the crossroads of death, is that not our desire? Is that not the duty of a son, the obligation of sons and daughters? We are Your sons and daughters who have that determination, so please do not let us forsake You on the path we walk. When we stand in places where we shed tears and can sigh in loneliness, may we first think of Your tears and first think of Your sighs, and may we be Your children who can live with all emotions centered on You.

When we think that all the stories coming from around the world are connected to our will, we cannot help but feel a sense of urgency that we cannot rest today. 

Let us bow down with our hands joined in prayer before Your holy sanctuary, staying up all night in holiness, worrying about Your will, worrying about Your work, and knowing that we have the mission to take responsibility for the mission of restoration. May we become Your sons and daughters who are worthy of receiving the names of loyal and virtuous ones in Your nation. We know that if there are many such sons and daughters in Korea, Korea can lead the world, so let us stand before this nation as Your sons and daughters who carry the spirit of Korea, called and sought by tradition. 

We earnestly request and desire that those who can become a substantial entity capable of resolving the past, present, and future in the world live here and lay the foundation for a new era. 

Let us become sons and daughters who can praise the value of today for tomorrow, and let us be sons and daughters who bow our heads and pray, pledging to dedicate tomorrow to You. We offer all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen. 

**Put forth your sincerity**
<Summary of the message> Many people who were at the forefront of history end up fading away in the end. Among you, those who are older have many accomplishments. Based on the present moment, is each person developing, stagnant, or retreating? You must belong to one of these three categories. If someone has been patriotic in their youth, even if they cannot be active in their old age, they must maintain a burning patriotism in their hearts to be a true patriot. If one gives up their patriotism in their heart just because they are old and regrets their patriotic sacrifices from their youth, then their past patriotic achievements will inevitably return to nothing. The traditional standards through a life of conviction must remain unchanged.

**You must work from an absolute position**
Now is not the time to bless the people of the spirit world. The return of earthly people is the priority. Therefore, even the pleas from the spirit world that cannot be expressed are set aside, and the providence of blessing is being carried out primarily for earthly people. Yet, those who cannot keep this important moment will be accused by the spirits. 

On December 8, 1968, at the former headquarters church. 
* This message was a special encouragement given to members who joined before 1963 after Sunday service, compiled from the second issue of the <Newsletter> (December 15, 1968) and notes recorded by the chairman of the Historical Compilation Committee, Yoo Kwang-ryeol. 

Those who have started anew centered around us are those who have been members for a long time. If someone entrusted with the will does not hold the will as absolute, that person can no longer be established before the will. Those who reminisce about the good old days are already pushed out of the benefits of this era. The time when you were loyal following the teacher should be different from the time when you are loyal yourself. In the past, the teacher was the one who restored the spiritual standard. However, from now on, you must inherit it and multiply it centered on yourselves. In other words, it is the time for actual restoration. Without a foundation for your activities, you cannot stand in an absolute position. The question is who will connect the spirit world of the elder nation, Cain, and the physical world of the younger nation, Abel.

Old members are trying to establish their positions. This is a very dangerous thing. God has not yet established His position either. For God to establish His position, at least a national standard that He can directly govern must be established. Therefore, you must abandon the desire to establish your position and continue to struggle with a heart full of longing.

Those who are loyal to God will be absolutely responsible for the teacher. If you cannot offer sincerity with your body in your old age, you must at least offer sincerity with your heart. If you leave behind successors who will inherit the will, God will recognize it.

**When you go to the spirit world**
When you arrive in the spirit world, you will be asked whether your current standard is more earnest than when you first faced the will. 

What if you die for the will? What will you achieve by living a miserable life for a thousand or ten thousand years? The Bible says, "Let us not become weary in doing good..." (Galatians 6:9). 

If those who belonged to the past era do not take the lead when a new era comes, they will become obstacles in history. Therefore, they will inevitably be removed. 

Blessed families have been blessed to carry out the mission of the second Messiah, but it has rather become a burden. When frost hits the path of the will, if you cannot fulfill your mission, the blessing will become a curse. Therefore, establishing positions is dangerous. If that establishment is for their own comfort, it is even more unacceptable.

When Cain and Abel arise in one household, judgment becomes necessary. There may arise situations where blessings must be given and then judgment must be made. Even from the current position, Cain and Abel are already forming.

Originally, when the teacher speaks joyful words centered on the will, heaven and earth should tremble with joy, and when he speaks sad words, heaven and earth should weep with lamentation. Originally, everyone who can come here should be Abel. To do so, you must absolutely obey the teacher's words.

Those who march for the nation's work will be stabbed to death if they are found drunkenly sobbing at an inn along the way.

**Let us put forth our sincerity**
The offering I bring must be pure and absolute. If you truly understand the will, you cannot sleep comfortably. You must go through trials to inherit the will. God sought a man who could fulfill His desire centered on Abel from the Adam family, but that desire was not fulfilled, and the providence extended for 4,000 years until Jesus came to the world.

Yet, even Jesus could not resolve that resentment. If a man could not resolve it, it goes without saying that a woman cannot. That is why women in the Unification Church must receive blessings and fulfill their responsibilities.

For 4,000 years, to find one man, they cried out, "Lord! Bridegroom, please come!" However, because Jesus came and could not fulfill His purpose and returned, countless Christians have been crying out, "Lord, come!" for the past 2,000 years while shedding blood.

If one understands the many twists of history caused by one woman's mistake, today’s women should feel an even greater sense of responsibility and repent. However, no matter how much women pray and strive, the purpose cannot be fulfilled until one man achieves victory.

In this age of the end, having gone through such a historical course of twists and turns, a new thing has finally emerged under the banner of the Unification Church, which has never happened in history. Therefore, the Unification Church is something that cannot be exchanged for the entirety of the world. Thus, the blessed families of the Unification Church must establish a new tradition. For one man to appear, countless people have shed blood for 6,000 years.
Many countries have emerged after being whipped. They staggered, trying to overcome the 6,000 years of Han, shedding tears they didn't even know they had, fulfilling God's will. Through this group, God has paved the way for a man to stand until now. He has given the gift of liberation, conferred the privilege of liberation, and blessed men to stand unconditionally in the place of liberation.

Blessed families have a connection that cannot be severed from the fortunes of heaven and earth. God has said that they are the ancestors who have been cherished for countless generations, the root of roots and the seed of seeds, wanting to place them in a precious position, which is the blessed family.

In other words, the couple that forms a blessed family transcends the origins of humanity's evil parents that were created by the fall of Adam and Eve in the Garden of Eden. They trace back to establish the standard of good parents and appear with the privileged gift of having the rights of good ancestors in a good world. Therefore, what makes that couple rejoice is also what makes heaven and earth rejoice. This is the kind of family that must exist.

You have likely met many spiritual witnesses who testify about the teacher. While many are curious as to why so many spiritual witnesses testify about the teacher, once they understand the truth, they cannot help but testify. There are tremendous issues hidden that you cannot comprehend.

There is only one path. The teacher has devoted 50 years to walk this path. From today, the label of 50 has been attached to the teacher. He prayed to God to quickly pass through the many 40 hills. Now that we are entering the 50 hills, what will we do during the 10 years leading to 60? We want to establish the tradition of the family and fulfill that mission.

The mission of the blessed family
Families exist for the will of God. Therefore, if there is no will, families will perish. Thus, those who want to live selfishly for their own families will ultimately fail, no matter how much they struggle. In the end, they can only follow the standards by which the Unification Church itself develops.

Such families cannot absolutely follow the standard of development centered on God. God does not exist for the development of such families or for the benefits of such families. However, families receive the benefits of the Unification Church; the Unification Church does not receive the benefits of families. What this means is that the teacher himself never thinks of receiving benefits from the blessed families he has established.

Men are like the right foot, and women are like the left foot. There should never be a conflict. The teacher speaks about families because families are sacred places, like the most holy sanctuaries. However, families are also fearsome places. When a family goes wrong, it completely ruins the future of their sons and daughters. If one side, either the man or the woman, excels, they can compensate for the other's shortcomings, but if both go wrong, it leads to complete ruin.

When a single seed is sown in the spring garden and germinates perfectly, it brings forth perfect fruit, but if it does not germinate, the seed itself disappears. In the family of Adam, Abel was established to seek the blessed family, and the same was true for Noah's family and Abraham's family. Therefore, the blessed families of the Unification Church must repent rather than just enjoy life.

The teacher also made his beloved wife suffer. He has endured hardships even while treating passing beggars with disdain. This is because the nation and the state have failed in their responsibilities. Therefore, no matter how lowly your position may be, you must act with the responsibility of a heavenly family. Just as a bride must uphold the traditions and laws of her husband's family, so too must you uphold the dignity and prestige of a blessed family, fulfilling your responsibilities while maintaining the heavenly traditions and laws.

How many families are there that uphold the dignity and prestige of a blessed family and fulfill their responsibilities by keeping the heavenly traditions and laws? Public families must establish the heavenly tradition and uphold it steadfastly, whether they are eating, walking, or breathing. Men and women must unite as one and must invest at least 40 years in special devotion.

The teacher has endured countless injustices before the nation for 40 years, carrying a deep-seated resentment in his bones while paving this path. Those who do not understand this will be accused before the teacher. They will also be accused before God for the efforts He has made over 6,000 years and Jesus over 2,000 years. When you think about the tremendous burden that lies behind this, can you sleep? Even three years of bathing in cold water and offering devotion is not enough.

You must have three children of faith
We have public laws. We must die for public matters and live publicly according to public standards. However, there are many rogues. We must awaken.

The teacher has commanded the regional leaders to observe the next three days as a heavenly holiday. However, yesterday, a certain leader from the Buddhist sect came to me, claiming that he received a message from the spirit world that today marks a holiday like no other in the world. This shows that we are all testifying to what we are doing. They even shared that certain individuals attended the recent Japan-Korea hunting competition and the Japan-Korea victory competition.

The time has come. The teacher has sacrificed his family until this day. It is not because he does not know how to love his family as much as you do, nor is it because he does not know how to manage his family as well as you do. It is because the nation and the church have failed, and this must be indemnified through the teacher's family. Knowing this, the teacher walks this path, enduring pain alone. If that is tradition, then the family must call upon the father, even while staggering, and run toward the final victory.

Blessed families must establish traditions. When viewed in light of the destiny of the Unification Church, families are internal. If they are internal, they must be disciplined. Therefore, even if our families scattered across the three thousand ri and the world become offerings, we must pray, "Father, please love your son. Please love all humanity!"

Just as Jesus prayed, "Abba Father, not my will, but yours be done," you too must pray that even if your son suffers, you will save and liberate all people. Yet, you remain oblivious. I have a son, but I cannot hold Seongjin and love him tenderly. This is because the principle of indemnity and restoration dictates that Abel cannot be determined without establishing Cain. Thus, when Cain is established, Abel must save Cain.

You are the same. You must understand the facts behind the baby in your womb. While you may rejoice and spend money at the birth of a child, that money should be spent for the sake of the will. The teacher has never been able to hold a 100-day celebration or an annual birthday celebration.

Even the baby in your womb must pass through three stages, so you must find three children of faith who represent Cain, allowing them to submit to the baby from the womb. Without doing so, you cannot love your own children. Just as the archangel served Adam and Eve while they were in the womb, you must establish three children of faith who represent Cain so that your children are served from the womb. There are these twists and turns on the path of the family.

Dictatorship connects with the best and with eternity. The absolute is the highest form of dictatorship. We must create a level ground even if it requires dictatorship. Thus, the mission of the family is tremendous. You must establish three children of faith in your family and organize them from the baby in the womb.

Baby in the womb! Hurry and be born. You must have children of faith who can do this. Otherwise, complete indemnity cannot occur.

The teacher has done such things over a seven-year course. Therefore, you must do the same until your child is over 20 and gets married. You must be able to sacrifice for your child and even give your life while still being grateful.

When viewed in light of Jesus, Peter, James, and John are the sons of Jesus. Under such principles, Jesus carried those three sons with him. That Jesus had to receive a bride as a groom and become a father. At that time, the three sons of faith, Peter, James, and John, hoped that the baby would be born quickly, and that baby had to be raised carefully until the age of 20 to marry without incident. They had to protect him so that the standard of Adam and Eve before the fall could be restored.

Practical application of the Principle
Because the relationship in which the archangel made a mistake before Adam and Eve in the Garden of Eden remains until later generations, we cannot sleep peacefully until we carefully raise and marry off our children of faith. This is because there is a possibility of falling. Only after carefully raising and blessing the children of faith can you be recorded as sons and daughters in God's lineage and be admitted into the kingdom of heaven.

You must understand that this principle exists. Restoration in the womb is absolute. That is why Cain and Abel fought, and Esau and Jacob struggled even in the womb. Thus, we seek to enter the womb.

You must serve in the opposite way from how you fought. Cain must serve Abel. If you cannot find this standard of service, complete restoration cannot occur. Because of this principle, God has been guiding for 6,000 years. What do you mean by believing and going to heaven? That is a misunderstanding of heaven. You must resolve these principled issues to receive liberation from the world of Satan.

To become children who lead the world, you must not deviate from this principle. You must lay this foundation. Therefore, at the very least, if you are a Unificationist, you must know what position you are in.

It is crucial for you to realize the principles through your principled life. So what is the realization of the principles? All other principles disappear, leaving only the principle of creation.

Because humans have a conscience, they can unite around the principle of creation. If one acts according to a good conscience, unity occurs automatically. Therefore, if you teach every day to hold onto your conscience and do only what your conscience approves, unity will happen automatically.

The conscience always accuses humans when they go in a bad direction. The conscience also plays a role in restraining bad actions. The conscience operates in everyone. So why does the conscience do this? That remains unknown. This conscience knows only two things: that bad is bad and good is good. It rejoices when things go well and feels sorrow when they go wrong. The conscience operates just like a natural phenomenon.

Without a subject and an object interacting, no power can arise. Power does not come from solitude. Power must arise from the subject and the object. When I say I am the object, even if I feel bad in my heart, there must be a subject, and even if I feel good, there must be a subject that can say it is good. This is why there is a term "sexual duality" in the principles of our Unification Church.

Where should people live? They should live in the most joyful places. They must live in the most ideal world. What kind of world is that? It is a place where people laugh, dance, and sing. It is a world where they live intoxicated by good winds. It is problematic if you cannot feel this in the Unification Church. Those who have never felt their cells laughing will become failures in the afterlife.

Our subject is God. Therefore, we must rejoice with God, sing with God, and dance with God. How wonderful would that be? Thus, our purpose is also God. Our life's journey is also a path to find God. That God is a realistic God.

The public is the gateway to heaven
Returning to the original position, think about why the heart can feel both sadness and joy. Unificationists must understand this. If there is a subject, there must be an object to complete the four-position foundation, and only then can the purpose of creation be fulfilled.

Therefore, you must have a sense of subjectivity. Unificationists must have a sense of subjectivity. In other words, everyone must have a thorough ideology, which is to have a sense of subjectivity. When this sense of subjectivity is for the nation and loves the nation, it becomes the standard for governing the nation.

This sense of subjectivity must have a positive form. Furthermore, it must not be isolated but must be established in a national context. It must be public, not private. Therefore, those who are loyal to the nation must set aside their private matters. Whether it is family, nation, or country, one must stand in a public position. You must stand in a public position and express your subjectivity from that perspective, acting from an absolute standpoint.

The public position refers to the heavenly principles. Why do we require a public standard? Because the public is the gateway to heaven. It is what the 30 million people of the nation and all humanity love. If you take that as a principle, even if you cannot act, you are still loved.

To have a sense of subjectivity, you must have an absolute sense of subjectivity. However, the absolute person, absolute righteousness, absolute goodness, and absolute love—all of these are subjects of God.

Therefore, your body and mind must become one with God, and your heart must become the subject, united with the body. Thus, my body, my self, must become a single subject. In other words, women and men must become one, just like a single cell, becoming a public subject.

When you stand in a public position, you must have the position of a couple. Thus, you become one with the public God and, transcending the nation, become one with everything in the world. When you become completely one before the perfect subject as a perfect object, the kingdom of heaven on earth will be realized.

In the future, how should Unificationists practice the principles in their lives? Unificationists must stand in a completely subjective position wherever they go. Then, everything they face becomes a perfect object, and they must regard and treat everything as if it were their own spouse. In other words, you must become a second teacher and pass through the standard of complete exchange to become a complete child of God. When that happens, you will achieve the complete four-position foundation and fulfill the purpose of creation.

Everything in this world can only exist through the law of the four-position foundation. The universe also exists centered on the law of give and take of the four-position foundation. Everything exists and develops centered on this law of the four-position foundation. Heavenly principles and the forces of the universe operate in this manner.

The causes of joy and sorrow
So where does a person feel the pangs of conscience? It is because the body moves even when the heart does not want it to. The subject, the heart, is not followed by the object, the body, which causes the heart to feel alienated from the body. When this happens, the standard of value diminishes and becomes smaller.

So where does joy come from? Joy arises when the body responds to the heart's demands.
When the mind and body become complete subjects and objects, achieving the principle of the Four Position Foundation, the body moves according to the desires of the mind. It is from this perspective that joy arises. As the heavenly fortune, which is the principle of the universe, supports us, the distance to meet God gradually shortens, bringing joy.  
However, when one engages in actions that weigh on their conscience, leading to the absence of the mind's counterpart, ultimately that subject will also cease to exist. The principle of this universe indicates that if only the subject exists, even if the object does not oppose, a force that drives it away will inevitably manifest. This appears as sorrow. Therefore, joy and sorrow arise from oneself as the cause.  
This universe began according to the laws of motion and the principles of the action of forces. Thus, everything aligns with the laws of heavenly fortune that match the rhythm of the universe. What aligns with the laws of heavenly fortune is the principle of the Four Position Foundation. Therefore, we must align ourselves with this principle of the Four Position Foundation and uphold it. However, if the results are lacking, one becomes a failure. In other words, no matter how well a couple gives and receives, if there are no children, the result is unhappiness. This is because the laws and principles of the universe revolve around the Four Position Foundation, and if only the Three Position Foundation is achieved, one is placed before the eternally revolving laws of the Four Position Foundation. When that happens, the distance from God increases, leading to natural sorrow.  
God is eternal. The reason we must have a sense of subjectivity is that God is eternal. Eternity means being free from any interference. It is not within the limits of the world of existence but exists beyond those limits. We seek to establish the value of existence to transcend that stage. Only when we have the authority to surpass the limits of the world of existence can we become one with God. Only then can we receive the guidance of God, who is the subject.  
For all things created by God to become one with Him, they must possess the ideological and emotional standards that allow God to guide them. When that happens, they become the perfect object before God, who is the complete subject governing this universe, and thus will inevitably progress and be able to dominate the world. However, to be eternally connected with God, it is not enough to have only strength. When one becomes completely one with the power of God's love, which is the action of God's servant, one cannot be separated or rejected eternally.  
Therefore, we must fight to center on God and connect with God's love. We must clearly understand that we should live a conscientious life and walk the path of struggle throughout our lives. To do this, we must realize a principled lifestyle. We must clearly distinguish between good and evil and live absolutely according to principles.  
From the perspective centered on conscience, if anything contributes even slightly to the standard of conscience, it brings joy, and if it detracts even slightly, it brings sorrow. Conscience commands us to always do good, as it moves according to the laws of heaven. Today, Unification Church members must absolutely avoid actions that weigh on their conscience. Conscience has a direct relationship with God, even more so than with others.  
It is unreasonable to say that one cannot walk the path of purpose because of someone else. In reality, one's own path is busy, and those they do not wish to see are organized by heavenly law. One should simply focus on walking their own path diligently. Satan supports the path of destruction, while God supports the path of prosperity. That is the turning point of good and evil, and the turning point of rise and fall.  
Thus, we must center on the principle of the Four Position Foundation and treat everything we encounter as if they were our own children. Such a mindset becomes the foundation upon which God can operate on this earth. This standard must be established starting from the family. Couples must unite their hearts. If the man is the subject, the woman must be the object, and they must completely give and receive. Spending a day, ten years, or a hundred years in this manner, when they finish their lives and go to the afterlife, those who lived in sorrow will go to hell, while those who had much joy will go to heaven. Thus, within our hearts, the lines of Satan and God coexist.  
In the world of philosophy, when the principle of unification reaches its peak, any political institution in the world must take a religious stance. Moreover, when considering the concept of restoration through indemnity, politics, academia, or anything else must adopt a religious perspective. Thus, many academic fields today are taking on a form of religion.  
Taking on the form of religion means rising from the very bottom. The Unification Church has also walked steps marked by a sorrowful historical fate while taking on the form of religion. So, what should we do by adopting the form of religion? We must resolve and develop the political, social, and academic issues of the world. To do this, we engage in the movement for church unity.  
And our proclamation of the victory ideology is because communism has become a major global issue today, and we must overthrow that communism. Therefore, our members have taken the initiative to establish the Victory Alliance, which has raised the standard to the highest level before our nation today. Currently, the movement for principle research is actively taking place on university campuses. Therefore, we must advance collectively. We must strengthen our victory activities. To defeat the communists, we must attack. In other words, we must take the offensive. We must conduct a nationwide and global advance centered on victory activities.  
In all areas, we must only advance.  
The activities on university campuses are responsible for the future generations, while victory activities are for the present. Religion is responsible for eternity. Therefore, we must advance in all areas. Within the church, we must establish a solid foundation by setting up familial, religious, and economic traditions. We must advance until 1970.  
If the nation falls, do you think your body and property will remain? We are all in a public position. When considering from a more valuable perspective, the individual must be sacrificed for the family, the family for the tribe, the tribe for the nation, the nation for the world. We must walk this public path to approach God, which is why the teacher is busy. No matter if individuals or everything else fails, the nation must not fall. Even if the nation falls, the world must not fall. Even if this earth fails, heaven must not fail. Therefore, those who do not comply with the teaching that the smaller must be sacrificed for the greater are all traitors.  
In the second seven-year course, three years are critical. Therefore, we must go forward with a more humble attitude, bowing our heads. Those who eat bad things and then eat good things are happy, but those who eat good things and then eat bad things are unhappy. Those who take the former position can be eternally happy.  
We must lay the foundation that can always leave good things behind. Moreover, since this year is a year of full advance, the members of the Unification Church must further solidify the church's traditions. We must also strengthen our principle research activities. If we do not make efforts and engage in activities in our respective fields, we cannot become Unification Church members.  
You must be fully mobilized to fulfill the heavenly mission in preparation for the crisis in Asia in 1970. Realizing that this is an urgent issue, you must devote yourself to being fully prepared, or you will not be able to stand before God. You must recognize that you are playing a leading role in establishing a new history and make new resolutions and determinations.
